She opens and operates a nightclub (the Frisco-themed venue, later the Jackpot establishment in subsequent runs); she does occasional acting work; she is consistently positioned as **professionally autonomous and romantically available but not pursuing**.

Behavioral notes from this era:

- **The Superior Spider-Man interval (Slott, 2012–2014).** Subject is briefly attracted to "Peter" during the Octavius occupation. She breaks it off because the man feels *wrong* in ways she cannot name. This is the file's most concrete confirmation of her unconscious pattern-reading: her social-cognition apparatus is fine-grained enough to detect a stranger inside a familiar body, and her exit reflex is fast enough to act on the signal before she can intellectualize it. **Confidence: high.** It is also, however, a self-undermining moment for her — she briefly doubts her own perception, which is rare for her and a stress signature worth flagging.
- **Parker Industries era (Slott, 2015–2017).** Subject rejoins Peter's professional orbit as an executive at his company. The relationship is professional-with-residue. Her competence in the corporate role is high; she manages his absences, runs interference with the board, and **slides back into the over-functioning posture under specific stress** — relapse-pattern, not characterological. When the company collapses, she extracts cleanly again.
- **The Mockingbird-adjacent observation.** Across this era multiple writers depict her as **friendly with other "superhero-adjacent women"** (Carlie Cooper before the falling-out, briefly Felicia Hardy in non-hostile registers, later the loose Jackpot crew). This is new. The marriage-era MJ had almost no female peer relationships of substance outside Aunt May. The post-reset MJ has begun to construct a peer bench. **This is, in clinical terms, the single healthiest development in her recorded history.**

## 4. The Spencer Run — Reconstruction, Stress-Test, Exit (2018–2021)

Nick Spencer's *Amazing Spider-Man* run is, for the purposes of this file, **the most extensive longitudinal behavioral dataset on Subject since the JMS era**, and the only one in which she is consistently written as a person with continuous interiority rather than as Peter's situational variable.

Key documented behaviors:

- **The reconciliation conversation (early Spencer issues).** Subject re-enters the relationship explicitly conditional. She names — out loud, to Peter — the historical pattern: *I run, you brood, we both pretend it's the situation, it isn't.* The naming-aloud capacity first observed in the JMS era is now fully established and operational. She is *using* the language of her own pathology to negotiate the relationship's terms. This is post-therapeutic behavior. There is no on-panel evidence she has been in therapy. The inference is that she has done the work informally, possibly across the editorial gap; either way, **the work is done and stable.**
- **Cohabitation, not marriage.** They live together. They do not re-marry. She does not raise it; he does not raise it. This is the new equilibrium and it is, by her standards, optimal: maximal intimacy, minimal legal/symbolic engulfment.
- **Tolerating the secret without absorbing it.** She is aware of Spider-Man activity, she is in proximity to it, she does not run her nervous system on it. When Peter is hurt, she nurses him; when he is on a case, she goes to bed. This is the **single largest affect-regulation upgrade** in her file. The marriage-era MJ ran a 24-hour threat-monitoring subroutine. The Spencer-era MJ has shut it off, or at least throttled it down to background process.
- **The Kindred / Mendel Stromm interval; the Paul Rabin departure.** When Peter — under circumstances she is not given full information about — breaks her trust (the issue 74 / 75 jump, the off-page extended absence, her relocation to an alternate dimension where she lives a parallel life with Paul Rabin and raises two children for an apparently subjective four years), her response is the cleanest exit of her published life. She does not punish, she does not threaten, she does not return. She just leaves. This is **the escalation ladder operating at its highest rung in its most mature form**: not the panicked geographic flight of 1978, not the dissociative captivity-PTSD exit of the Mackie era, but a calm, articulated, *I am not available for this* departure.

**The Rabin episode itself** is a critical somatic and psychological event. She lived, by her own experienced time, four years as a wife and mother to children who are biologically hers in that pocket reality. She bonded with them. She lost them when the reality collapsed and only she and Rabin (and the children, in a complicated displaced sense) emerged. *The reactivation of the perinatal-loss vulnerability is total.* That she did not collapse but instead built a public romantic life with Rabin and held it together for the Wells run's opening issues is **prognostically extraordinary** and also exactly what the file would predict: suppression is her superpower, and she has just had to run it at maximum draw.

## 5. The Wells Run and Current State (2022–Present)

Zeb Wells's ongoing *Amazing Spider-Man* run picks up with Subject living with Paul Rabin, raising two children (presented in the public-facing reality as Rabin's from a prior relationship; in the deeper continuity as the children she bore in the pocket reality). Peter is estranged, hurt, blocked from explanation. Subject is, on the surface, **the most stable she has been in her published life**.

The file's read on what is *actually* happening:

- **The Rabin relationship is a stabilization scaffold, not a destination.** Rabin is competent, kind, professionally accomplished (an architect / inventor profile), and — critically — **does not have a secret identity, does not attract lethal stalkers, and does not require her to manage his survival.** He is, in the terms of her stated needs, exactly what she has said for forty publication-years she should want. The fact that the relationship reads, on panel, as *correct but not animated* is the diagnostic data. She has selected the safe option after the most acute trauma cycle of her life. This is a **regulation-phase pairing**, the relational equivalent of a convalescent diet.
- **The children are the load-bearing attachment.** Whatever ambiguities the Wells run leaves in the air about Rabin himself, Subject's behavior with the children is **unguarded in a way nothing else in her file is.** This is the perinatal wound resolving in real time, against odds, through the only mechanism that could resolve it: actual experienced parenthood, even if metaphysically peculiar. The file flags this as **the most psychologically significant active process in her life.**
- **The estrangement from Peter is genuine and is also incomplete.** When they are in scenes together, her affect is controlled but not absent. The old reading-of-the-room capacity is still online; she knows what he is feeling, she chooses not to act on it. *She is enforcing the boundary, not having ceased to feel.* The distinction matters. A subject who had genuinely concluded the relationship would not need to enforce — she would have nothing to enforce against. The enforcement is the tell.
- **Her professional life is the quietest it has been since the Slott club years.** Acting work is intermittent; she is, functionally, in a domestic phase. This is the first time in her recorded life she has accepted **domesticity without it being framed as a sacrifice or a compromise**. Whether this is sustainable for her is the open question and the file's primary current uncertainty.

## 6. Current-State Synthesis (as of last update)

**Residence.** New York metropolitan area, cohabiting with Paul Rabin and the two children. Domicile is upper-middle-class, design-forward (Rabin's professional aesthetic predominates; her own presence in the décor is observable but secondary — *she has not yet imprinted on the space*, which is itself a signal).

**Daily routine, inferred.** School run; coffee; intermittent agent / casting calls; gym or yoga (low confidence, but consistent with documented somatic-maintenance habits from earlier eras); evening with the children; relatively early sleep. The party-girl chronotype of the Lee/Romita era and the late-night club operator chronotype of the Slott era are both **discontinued**. She is keeping a parent's schedule and appears to find it restorative rather than constraining.

**Substance baseline.** Tobacco: not currently observed; assume in remission, with stress-contingent relapse risk. Alcohol: light social, no observed escalation. No other substance use on record.

**Affective baseline.** Constricted-but-stable. The brightness she could turn on like a stage light in earlier eras is **dialed down and used selectively**. She is not performing for the camera of the room as constantly as she once did. This is either maturity or a low-grade flattening; the file's read is **mostly the former with some of the latter** — she has paid in muted affect for the right to actually feel what she actually feels, and she has, on the available evidence, decided the trade is worth it.

**Threat exposure.** Substantially reduced from peak. Rabin is not a target. The children, at present, are not targets. Peter's enemies are not currently her enemies in the way they were during the marriage. This is the **lowest threat-exposure baseline of her adult life** and her nervous system is, observably, beginning to recalibrate to it. Hypervigilance signatures (startle response, sleep architecture) appear to be remitting, though under any reactivation they would return rapidly.

**Vulnerabilities, current.**
1. **The Rabin relationship's metaphysical instability.** She built it on a foundation she does not fully understand and that the narrative will, at some point, force her to confront. When it does, the perinatal-loss reactivation will be severe.
2. **The Peter question is unresolved, not closed.** She has not concluded the relationship; she has paused it. A resumption is, on the established pattern, a matter of time and conditions, not of possibility.
3. **The children as new pressure point.** She now has, for the first time in her life, attachments she cannot exit from without destroying herself. The exit strategy that has been her keel since age twelve is, regarding them, **unavailable**. She has not yet had to confront what her psychology does when its primary defense is removed.

**Strengths, current.**
1. Articulacy about her own patterns is at lifetime high.
2. Peer-bench (female friends, professional contacts, the loose Jackpot-adjacent network) is broader than at any previous era.
3. Substance and affect regulation in remission/stable.
4. **For the first time, she is in a life that does not require her defenses to run at full draw.** Whether she can tolerate the unfamiliarity of safety is the live question.

**Prognosis.** Cautiously favorable. The trajectory from the avoidant-flight teenager of the Conway backstory to the calmly-departing partner of the Spencer run to the domestically-stabilized parent of the Wells run is, viewed longitudinally, **one of the more successful self-driven psychological integration arcs in the file room**. She has done what most subjects in her diagnostic vicinity never do: she has named the pattern, modified it, and built a life shaped around the modification rather than the original wound. The remaining work — the unresolved Peter attachment, the latent perinatal material, the untested question of whether she can stay when staying is the harder thing than leaving — is real, but it is the work of a person who has demonstrated, over five published decades, that she is capable of doing it.

**Surveillance recommendation.** Maintain passive observation. Flag for re-tasking on any of the following triggers: pregnancy, infant proximity beyond the existing children, any Osborn-family reactivation, any documented contact with Peter Parker exceeding two consecutive scenes of unguarded affect, any geographic move out of the metropolitan area, resumption of tobacco use. Absent triggers, this subject is **not currently in a phase requiring intervention or escalation**. She is, by the standards of her own life, well.

*End Chronology IV. Section closes pending next canonical update.*


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — SUBJECT: MARY JANE WATSON-PARKER

*Compiled longitudinally from observed canonical record; somatic inferences extrapolated from depicted symptomatology, recurrent stress signatures, and the cumulative trauma load of a non-powered civilian embedded in the orbit of a top-tier costumed combatant for ~25 in-story years. This section reads the body — what it has carried, what it has metabolized, and what it stores against her wishes.*

---

## 1. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE

**Demographics.** Adult human female, baseline unenhanced physiology. Documented height in the 5'8"–5'9" range; long-limbed, narrow through the shoulders and hips, low resting body fat — a build maintained by occupational demand (modeling/runway/on-camera work) rather than by athletic conditioning per se. Hair: natural red, occasionally chemically refreshed during sustained professional engagements; documented across multiple writers as a defining somatic signature, with at least one observed period of cutting and dyeing as a self-presentation reset following relational rupture.

**Cardiopulmonary baseline.** No documented cardiac history; no documented pulmonary disease prior to tobacco recruitment (see §4). Aerobic capacity above population median by occupational necessity — dance training in adolescence (the go-go era in the early ASM appearances was not affectation; she could actually do it), maintained intermittently by stage and on-set physical demand. She runs when she has to and does not gas out fast; her flight reflex, examined somatically, is a *trained* flight reflex.

**Musculoskeletal.** No congenital pathology. Long-term low-grade postural strain consistent with chronic modeling work — held positions, asymmetric loading, footwear-induced gait compromise. Probable subclinical cervical and lumbar tension; the on-panel record shows her reaching for her neck and rolling her shoulders during high-load conversations far more often than during ordinary scenes, a tell consistent with somatized stress holding.

**Neurological baseline.** Intact. No documented TBI despite multiple kidnappings and at least one survived plane crash, which is statistically improbable and should be flagged as either canonical convenience or genuine luck. Reflexes, gait, and fine motor function appear unimpaired throughout the record. Sensorium grossly intact.

**Endocrine / reproductive baseline.** Menarche presumed normal-timed (no flashback indicates otherwise). One full-term pregnancy (see §3). No documented thyroid, adrenal, or metabolic disorder, though chronic stress load over decades raises the prior on subclinical HPA-axis dysregulation — the insomnia/appetite-loss pattern (§4) is consistent with this.

**Dermatological.** Unremarkable except for occupational concerns: cumulative cosmetic load over a long modeling career, periodic stage-makeup dermatitis inferred from a handful of off-shift depictions of bare-faced skin in subtly worse condition than her on-camera face. No tattoos in mainline continuity. No documented scarring from her many adult exposures, which — again — strains plausibility and is the kind of detail an actual surveillance file would flag as either cosmetically managed or charitably under-depicted.

---

## 2. DEVELOPMENTAL & ADOLESCENT MEDICAL HISTORY

**Childhood.** No documented major illness. The relevant medical history of her childhood is *environmental*: a household with intermittent paternal verbal aggression and at least implied physical aggression, an itinerant residential pattern (Pittsburgh → Philadelphia → Queens), and food/sleep regularity that can be inferred to have been irregular during the unstable interregnum between her mother's departure and the settlement with Aunt Anna. The somatic consequences of this kind of childhood — elevated baseline sympathetic tone, foreshortened sleep architecture, hyper-attuned startle threshold — are present in her adult presentation and almost certainly seeded here.

**Adolescence.** Performance-driven; dance and theater commitments suggest the typical adolescent-performer injury profile (ankle sprains, shin splints, minor overuse) but nothing has surfaced on the record as a chronic complaint. Reproductive and sexual health: the canon is appropriately silent; nothing suggests pathology. The character is depicted as having had a more active dating life than Peter prior to their first meeting, which is socially documented rather than medically relevant except as it establishes a baseline pattern of using sexual and romantic engagement as social currency rather than as primary affective channel.

**Late adolescence — the witnessing event.** The night she observed Peter Parker exit the Parker home in costume after Uncle Ben's death is not a medical event in the conventional sense, but it loaded a secret-keeping burden onto a nervous system already optimized for vigilance. The body cost of carrying that secret in isolation, for the time she carried it, should be entered into the longitudinal stress ledger as a chronic low-grade allostatic load distinct from any single trauma.

---

## 3. OBSTETRIC HISTORY

**Pregnancy (Clone Saga era).** One pregnancy, carried to apparent term. Antenatal course depicted as broadly unremarkable in terms of maternal physiology — no preeclampsia, no documented gestational diabetes, no hyperemesis beyond ordinary depiction. Psychologically the pregnancy was a high-load event (see §6); somatically it was, on the available evidence, normal.

**Delivery and outcome.** Apparent stillbirth at delivery (in-universe truth: neonatal abduction by Norman Osborn; subject's *lived* medical experience was perinatal loss with no body, no answers, no funeral she could organize her grief around). This is the single most consequential entry in her obstetric file. The standard medical sequelae of perinatal loss — postpartum hormonal cascade uncoupled from infant care, lactation onset and suppression, uterine involution in the absence of nursing, sleep architecture disruption without the infant-cued counterweight — all occurred in her body without the social and clinical scaffolding that ordinarily attends grief support. There is no on-panel evidence she received adequate postpartum follow-up; her depicted return to function is suspiciously fast, which medically reads as suppression, not recovery.

**Sequelae.** No documented subsequent pregnancy in mainline continuity. Flinch responses to infant-coded stimuli are observable across multiple subsequent writers, particularly in scenes involving Aunt May's friends' grandchildren and one notable depiction of her freezing momentarily at a baby-shower scene during the late Michelinie/early Mackie transition. Whether she is reproductively capable of another pregnancy is medically unaddressed and personally unprobed by her on the record. This is not an oversight; it is a *choice*, and an avoidance.

**Alternate-continuity confirmations.** *Renew Your Vows* depicts a successfully carried subsequent pregnancy and a healthy daughter (Annie); her maternal somatic and behavioral function in that universe is unimpaired, suggesting that the mainline avoidance is psychological rather than physiological in origin.

---

## 4. SUBSTANCE HISTORY

**Tobacco.** Documented onset in the late Michelinie/DeMatteis era as an acute relapse rather than a first initiation — the dialogue makes clear she had smoked previously, quit, and resumed under marital stress. Pattern: stress-contingent, never social, never recreational. She smokes when the suppression strategy is failing, and the cigarette functions as a deliberate respiratory intervention — slow inhalation, breath-holding, exhalation — that is, functionally, a vagal-tone hack she taught her own body before she could have named it as such. DeMatteis's depiction is unusually careful: she smokes alone, usually at a window, usually after Peter has left for patrol. The behavior reads as both nicotinergic anxiolysis and as a private ritual of separateness — a few minutes of being a self that is not managing him.

Tobacco use appears in remission across post-OMD continuity. Whether this represents genuine cessation or editorial sanitization is ambiguous; the underlying anxiety substrate has not been removed, so the relapse risk under reactivating stress should be considered nonzero.

**Alcohol.** Social-to-moderate baseline. Cocktail-comfortable, wine-with-dinner, never depicted intoxicated in a sustained way. At least one observed episode of recruiting alcohol to dull acute distress — drinking alone, slowly, after the separation arc kicked off; another implied use during the post-Gwen mourning period in the early Conway run, though there she was at least drinking in company. No documented dependence, no withdrawal, no functional impairment. The clinically notable feature is not the quantity but the *function* — when she drinks alone, it is doing work, not company.

**Cannabis / other recreational.** No documented use. The era of her first appearances coded her as discotheque-adjacent rather than counterculture-adjacent, which is a meaningful distinction; she was performing on the surface of the late-60s scene, not embedded in its pharmacology.

**Prescription medication.** Not depicted on the record. Given her sleep-onset insomnia during the stalker arc and the separation arc, the prior on at least episodic prescribed hypnotic use is high; the absence from canon is more likely a writers'-room omission than a clinical fact. No evidence of misuse.

**Caffeine.** High baseline, consistent with the modeling/acting schedule and chronic sleep debt. Observable across decades as a consistent prop in scenes set before noon.

---

## 5. TRAUMA EXPOSURES — CATALOGUED

This file would be incomplete without an itemized exposure ledger. The subject's cumulative trauma load is comparable to that of a longtime hostage-family-member or a war correspondent's spouse, with the additional feature that her primary attachment figure is *himself* a recurring source of her traumatic exposure.

**Childhood/developmental:** verbal/emotional abuse from father (chronic, multi-year, with at least one depicted instance of physical aggression toward her mother in her presence); abandonment-by-departure of mother with daughters; parentification by her sister's family-of-procreation collapse; one acute flight event (her own departure from her sister's household).

**Adult — kidnappings and hostage events** (non-exhaustive, in approximate canonical order): Hobgoblin (multiple); Venom (the home-invasion event in particular, which is a category of trauma — *the bedroom breached* — distinct from public abduction); Chameleon (multiple, with identity-deception elements that compound the trauma); Mysterio; Norman Osborn (multiple, with the additional trauma of personal targeting); the prolonged captivity during the plane-crash/separation arc, which functioned as effectively a months-long isolation event with intermittent threat exposure.

**Adult — environmental disasters:** the plane crash (depicted as a near-death event with brief loss of consciousness implied); proximity exposure to multiple superhuman-scale combat events at close range, with all the percussive, thermal, and particulate exposures that implies; at least one structure-fire exposure.

**Adult — interpersonal:** the stalker arc (Michelinie), which produced acute anxiety symptoms (see §6) and functioned as a sustained-threat event rather than a discrete trauma; the assault during that arc that culminated in the on-panel collapse; betrayals and reveals in the post-OMD continuity that, while psychologically rather than physically injurious, register on the body as ruptures.

**Cumulative load.** The relevant medical observation is that she is functional. By the standards of her exposure profile she ought to be visibly impaired, and she is not. This is partly resilience, partly defense efficiency (see Psychiatric), and partly — clinically — *unprocessed*. The body keeps the score even when the person declines to read it.

---

## 6. SOMATIC STRESS SIGNATURES — LONGITUDINAL

This is the section of the file most worth attending to, because it is where her affective strategy and her body diverge.

**Sleep.** Baseline sleep architecture appears foreshortened — she is depicted across decades as awake when Peter returns from patrol, awake before he wakes, awake reading at 2 AM. During acute stress arcs the foreshortening becomes frank insomnia: sleep-onset latency increased, mid-cycle waking, early-morning arousal she does not return from. The stalker arc, the separation arc, and the post-OMD ruptures all show the same pattern. She does not, on the record, complain about it; she manages it with caffeine and with task.

**Appetite.** Stress-suppressed rather than stress-driven. Under load she does not eat; the DeMatteis dialogue is explicit about weight loss during one stretch, and the visual record across several artists tracks consistent thinning during high-stress arcs. This is medically a vulnerability — it removes a metabolic buffer she has little of to begin with.

**Headache.** Tension-pattern headaches referenced in dialogue and depicted as hand-to-temple gestures with high frequency during arcs involving Peter's secret-life leakage into her professional life. Consistent with cervicogenic and stress-driven tension headache. No migrainous features depicted.

**Startle.** Elevated. The JMS run depicts this most clearly — she startles at sudden window movement, at unexpected entries, at phones ringing late. This is a learned response to her exposure history and is functionally adaptive in her actual environment, which is a feature of her medical picture rather than a bug.

**Autonomic.** Episodes consistent with panic — tachycardia, hyperventilation, paresthesias — depicted at least twice (the climax of the stalker arc, and a quieter episode during the separation arc in a bathroom mirror scene). Frequency low; ceiling high; recovery fast. She does not have a panic disorder; she has panic-spectrum events under specific provocations.

**Dissociative.** Derealization and depersonalization episodes documented across the captivity/separation arc and intermittently in the JMS run. Brief, situation-bound, ego-syntonic at the time and ego-dystonic after. This is the somatic correlate of her psychological flight reflex — when she cannot leave the room, her perception leaves it for her.

**GI.** Inferred rather than documented; the appetite suppression and the substance recruitment pattern both suggest at least functional dyspepsia during high-load periods.

**Menstrual.** Off-panel. Given the stress and weight-fluctuation profile, intermittent oligomenorrhea would be unsurprising. Not documented.

---

## 7. TRANSFORMATIONS, IMPERSONATIONS, AND IDENTITY-LEVEL EVENTS

She has not, on the mainline record, undergone superhuman transformation. She has, however, been subject to a category of events with no civilian analogue and meaningful medical relevance:

- **Sustained impersonation by Chameleon** and others — i.e., periods during which someone else was inhabiting her social role while she was held elsewhere. The medical relevance is reentry trauma: returning to a life one's body did not live for some weeks produces a documented dissociative load that she has navigated multiple times.
- **Apparent death events** — she has been believed dead by her primary attachment figure on multiple occasions, and has had to manage the somatic and relational fallout of resurrection-from-presumed-death. This is rare in the general medical population and common in hers.
- **Symbiote proximity** — at least one documented close exposure to the Venom symbiote in domestic space, with the attendant acute fear response and (per later canon) low-grade conditioned aversion to symbiote-coded stimuli.
- **Brief alternate-continuity transformations** (House of M, etc.) which are not load-bearing on her mainline medical history but should be flagged in any longitudinal file.

No surgical history is documented. No prosthetics, implants, or chronic device dependencies. No documented allergies. Blood type unestablished on the record.

---

## 8. PSYCHOLOGICAL IMPACT — INTEGRATED PER EXPOSURE

Each entry above carries a psychological tail, and the file's purpose is to map them:

- **Childhood verbal abuse** → primary attachment architecture; reaction-formation defense; the lifelong refusal to be seen crying.
- **Family-of-origin flight** → permanent guilt-debt; the flight reflex itself as both adaptive skill and recurring liability.
- **Witnessing Peter change** → the eighteen-year secret-keeping load; chronic vigilance baseline elevation.
- **Gwen Stacy's death (proximate)** → the laugh-at-the-funeral episode; first observable adult instance of manic defense under bereavement.
- **First proposal/flight** → consolidation of approach-then-bolt as her engaged-attachment pattern.
- **Marriage** → integration attempt; partial success; somatic stress signatures intensify as she absorbs more of Peter's load.
- **Stalker arc** → acute anxiety presentation; first depicted panic-spectrum episode; tobacco relapse anchor.
- **Perinatal loss** → suppression as primary strategy; durable infant-stimulus aversion; the single most under-processed entry in her file.
- **Plane crash and captivity** → derealization onset; the somatic permission to finally exit the marriage; PTSD-spectrum symptoms most fully expressed here.
- **JMS reconciliation** → first sustained period of integrated functioning; somatic markers improve when the secret-keeping load is shared with Aunt May.
- **Post-OMD continuity** → boundary competence increases; somatic stress signatures depicted at lower intensity; relapse risks (tobacco, dissociative episodes, flight) remain latent but unactivated.

---

## 9. SUMMARY MEDICAL FORMULATION

The subject is a constitutionally healthy adult female carrying the cumulative somatic load of a developmental trauma profile, a high-exposure adult life, and one unresolved perinatal loss, who has organized her physiology around a single dominant strategy: *do not let the body show what the self has decided not to feel.* The strategy is highly effective and incompletely successful. The receipts are in her sleep, her appetite, her startle, her cigarettes-at-windows, and the small involuntary hand-to-temple that even her best writers cannot help giving her when the conversation gets close. She is, medically, what a person looks like when they have spent forty years winning the argument with their own nervous system on points, never by knockout. The file's standing recommendation is that any future arc involving pregnancy, infant proximity, or a return of Osborn-coded stimuli be treated as medically — not only psychologically — destabilizing, and that her tobacco-relapse threshold under acute marital stress be considered low.

End medical history. Forwarded for cross-reference with Psychological and Psychiatric sections.


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — SUBJECT: MARY JANE WATSON

*Classification: Total-surveillance physical record. Every datum below is either canon-observable across published depiction (Romita Sr., Andru, Romita Jr., Bagley, Larsen, Buscema, Sal Buscema on Spectacular, Mark Bagley & Mike Wieringo on Sensational, JRJR on JMS, Bachalo, Dodson, Ramos, Pichelli, Ottley, Coipel, Bachalo again on Spencer) or extrapolated at the granular level a continuous surveillance file would actually contain. Cross-state shifts noted throughout: C = calm baseline; S = ambient stress; T = threat-recognized; I = intimacy/private; X = breaking-point/exit-imminent.*

---

## 1. ANTHROPOMETRY & STANDING SIGNATURE

Approximately 5'8" barefoot, long-limbed, narrow through the shoulder relative to hip, the build that reads as "model" before any styling is added — a fact she has weaponized, exploited, and resented at different developmental stages. Weight has fluctuated visibly across canon in a narrow band tracking emotional load: gaunter through the stalker arc (Michelinie), the separation arc (Mackie), and the Spencer-era estrangement; fuller and visibly healthier across the JMS reconciliation and the Renew-Your-Vows continuity, where she is permitted to eat without monitoring herself. The fluctuation itself is the data point — body weight is a downstream readout of how much of herself she is currently performing.

Resting posture in **C** is upright but not military: weight on one hip, opposite knee soft, one shoulder a half-inch lower than the other in a long-trained model's contrapposto she has long since stopped doing on purpose. In **S** the weight redistributes evenly, both feet plant, the contrapposto disappears — she is no longer presenting, she is *bracing*. In **T** the chin drops two degrees, the chest hollows a finger's-width, and she squares to whatever the threat is rather than turning sideways; this is the Queens girl beneath the cover. In **I** the spine softens through the lumbar; she will lean into furniture, into doorframes, into the man, in a way she does not allow herself anywhere else. In **X** the posture is the most legible tell in the entire file: she goes very, very still, both feet flat, hands quiet, shoulders dropped — the body of someone who has already decided to leave and is only waiting for the conversation to end.

---

## 2. GAIT, TRANSIT, AND THE WAY SHE TAKES UP A ROOM

Walks with a long stride and a slight forward lean, heel-strike audible in heeled boots — she favors a low block heel for daily wear and only goes higher for work or armor. The hips do not exaggerate; the swing is generated at the shoulder, a dancer's habit retained from the late-sixties Romita era when she was, on panel, go-go dancing weekly. She *enters* rooms — door pushed with the flat of the hand, eyes up and scanning before the body fully crosses the threshold, smile pre-loaded by the time anyone could have registered her. This entrance is reflexive and pre-cognitive; she does it in empty rooms.

In **C** she takes routes through interiors that maximize sightlines: she will cross a kitchen along the counter rather than the open floor, will sit with her back to a wall and her face to the door, will pick the barstool nearest the exit. In **S** the route-finding tightens — she will not stand in the center of a room; she gravitates to vertical surfaces. In **T** her gait shortens by perhaps fifteen percent and the lead foot lands flat instead of heel-first, a quietening adjustment that produces a markedly less audible walk; she does this without conscious thought, and Peter has remarked on it more than once across the canon (the "I didn't hear you come in" beat is a recurring panel). In **I**, alone with him, her transit is the loosest it ever is — bare feet, scuff of the sole on hardwood, sometimes a half-skip on the turn. In **X** she walks *normally* on the way out the door, and that normality is the warning.

---

## 3. THE HAIR

Operationally the most documented surface of her body, because it is the surface she has used as semaphore for fifty years of publication. Natural color is the deep, saturated red attested from first appearance; she has cycled through a documented short crop (Bagley/Larsen era, post-pregnancy-loss — a textbook trauma haircut she explicitly did not explain), an asymmetric bob (Mackie separation arc), the long waves of the JMS reconciliation, and the businesslike shoulder-length of the Spencer run.

Handling tells, in granular order of frequency:

- **Tucking right side behind right ear with the second and third fingers** — her single most frequent gesture. Reads as flirtation; functions as a self-soothing pacifier and a thinking-tic. Frequency in **C**: every two to four minutes in conversation. In **S**: increases to nearly continuous. In **T**: stops entirely.
- **Two-handed lift off the nape, hold, drop** — a heat/overwhelm release. Appears under physical heat (kitchen, summer) and under social heat (argument). The hold-duration is the meter: under three seconds is comfort, over five is *I need this conversation to stop*.
- **Twisting a single lock around the index finger** — appears only when she is genuinely thinking, not when she is performing thinking. Worth flagging as a rare *honest* tell.
- **Sweeping the whole mass over one shoulder** — pre-photograph, pre-kiss, pre-confrontation; an arming gesture.
- **Letting it fall completely across the face, head bowed** — appears only in **X**, and almost only when she is alone or believes herself alone. The single most accurate visual readout of her actual interior state.

In **I** she lets him put his hands in it; she does not allow this from anyone else and has flinched, on panel, from professional stylists touching the back of her neck. The neck-touch flinch is a documented stress-response and may key to Osborn-arc captivity.

---

## 4. FACE — MICROEXPRESSION INVENTORY

The face is her primary instrument and the file's richest single surface.

**Baseline smile (C):** asymmetric, left corner higher than right by perhaps two millimeters, eyes narrowed at the outer canthus — a real Duchenne smile she can produce at will, which is the unusual professional skill of an actor and which makes her almost impossible to read by smile alone. She has had this smile since first appearance and uses it as a social opener the way other people use a handshake.

**Performance smile:** wider, more symmetric, teeth fully visible, *eyes not engaged* — orbicularis oculi does not fire. Deployed at industry events, with press, with strangers, and — telling — with Peter when she is concealing something. Distinguishable to a trained observer; not to him until the JMS run, when she explicitly teaches him to see it.

**The eyebrow lift:** single right brow, often paired with a tilted head. Used to disarm, to flirt, and — most often — to *deflect a question she will not answer*. Frequency increases sharply when a topic approaches her family of origin.

**The eye-narrow with mouth-corner-down:** her actual calculating face, which she allows out maybe twice an issue and almost never on camera at a work event. This is the face of the person who clocked Peter's identity from a single window.

**The blink-rate baselines:** elevated in **C** (she is performing engagement); *drops* in **S** and **T** to a near-stare; *drops further* in **X** to the slow, deliberate blink of someone who has stopped processing the room and is processing only her own decision.

**The jaw:** masseter visible on tension, especially during arguments with Peter about disclosure or risk. She has, in multiple depictions, clenched hard enough through long scenes to produce tension headaches she does not mention until the next morning.

**The cry:** rare on-panel and almost always partial — eyes wet, no sound, one hand to the mouth, head turned away. She has the Conway-attested resolution from childhood (*never let anyone see her cry*) and she largely keeps it. The full cries are landmarks: Gwen's funeral (delayed, alone), the proposal refusal (alone), the lost pregnancy (suppressed almost entirely on panel; one tear, then function resumed), the JMS-era confessional scenes (allowed, with effort), the Spencer betrayal (allowed, then immediate exit). She does not cry when she is going to leave.

---

## 5. HANDS

Long-fingered, kept short-nailed when she is working (acting, modeling — the industry hates long nails on a take), grown out and lacquered in deep red or wine when she is not. The lacquer color is itself a state indicator: red is **C/I**, neutral is **S**, bare-and-short is recovery.

Hand habits:
- **The cigarette grip (DeMatteis era, intermittent relapse).** Held between index and middle at the second knuckle, elbow tucked, exhale to the side and up. She does not take the cigarette to her mouth — she brings her mouth to the cigarette, a small leftward neck dip. The relapse is invariably stress-keyed and she invariably quits again within weeks without commentary.
- **Glass-handling.** Wine glass at the stem, never the bowl; tumbler with all four fingers wrapped, thumb on the rim — the second grip appears only at home, only after a hard day, and she will turn the glass a quarter-revolution on the table between sips. This rotation count is a near-perfect proxy for how much she is not saying.
- **The wedding ring (marriage era, mainline and Renew Your Vows).** Worn on the correct finger; she turns it inward toward the palm when she goes out without Peter, an unconscious privacy gesture rather than a deceptive one. Removed and replaced on the nightstand with a specific small *click* that he learned to listen for.
- **Touching her own throat.** Two fingers to the suprasternal notch when surprised, three fingers flat across the collarbone when listening to something she finds moving, full hand to the side of the neck under genuine threat — a graded self-protective ladder she runs without awareness.
- **Touching him.** Back of his neck (proprietary, public), small of his back (steering, public), inside of his wrist (private check-in, **I**), palm flat to his sternum (the *stop talking* gesture she developed across the marriage), thumb to the corner of his mouth (post-conflict reconciliation, **I** only).

She does not point. She gestures with an open palm or with the chin. The no-pointing rule is consistent across every artist and every decade and may date to a paternal prohibition — Philip Watson is the right age and disposition to have hit a daughter's hand for it.

---

## 6. VOICE

Mezzo, smoke-roughened in the DeMatteis years, recovered after. Trained — the acting career put her through diction work that is audible in her enunciation of final consonants; she does not drop a *t*. Three operative registers:

- **Public:** bright, a quarter-step higher than her natural pitch, laugh deployed at the ends of her own sentences as punctuation.
- **Private (C/I):** lower, slower, less laugh, more pause. The pause is the diagnostic feature — she allows silence she would never allow in public.
- **Stressed (S/T/X):** flatter, evenly paced, almost affectless. When her voice goes *level* the file should escalate, not relax. Her father's voice rose when he was angry; she trained the opposite. Peter has learned, by the JMS run, that the flat voice is the alarm bell.

The laugh: three distinct.
1. **Social laugh** — head back, throat open, audible from across a room. A tool.
2. **Real laugh** — closer to a single exhale, head ducked, hand toward but not touching her mouth, often paired with a small headshake. Rare; almost exclusively at Peter, May, or her own genuine surprise.
3. **The inappropriate laugh** — the documented Gwen-funeral laugh, a brittle high-pitched escape under affective overload. Appears two or three times across canon and is always a *warning* of imminent decompensation, never an expression of amusement.

She has, on panel, *sung* — well enough to suggest training, though she downplays it. She hums while cooking. She does not whistle.

---

## 7. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

Baseline a six-to-seven hour sleeper, late-to-bed and slow-to-rise, with a long pre-sleep wind-down ritual that includes face wash, the specific brush-out of the hair into a single loose plait, and (marriage era) a check on whether Peter is in the bed beside her. The check is the load-bearing element: if he is absent, she will not sleep deeply, only surface-doze, and will rise at first sound from the fire escape.

Disturbance signatures:
- **Stalker arc (Michelinie):** documented insomnia, hypervigilance, repeated waking, the artist depicts her sitting upright at the window in the middle of the night — a body posture sustained long enough to be observed by Peter and to read as exhaustion in following panels.
- **Plane crash / captivity recovery:** night terrors implied by depiction; she does not name them. She begins sleeping with a light on, then with the bedroom door open.
- **JMS era reconciliation:** the best-attested sleep period of the file — back to baseline, long stretches, the loose plait returns.
- **Spencer-era estrangement:** alone, she sleeps poorly; depicted with takeout containers and a laptop open at 3 a.m.

She sleeps curled on her left side, knees drawn up, one hand under the pillow, one across her own ribs — a self-holding posture that does not change whether or not the bed is shared. In **I** she will sleep against him, but the self-holding hand remains across her own body. She does not give that hand away.

---

## 8. EATING

Trained, by industry and by upbringing, to eat in front of others as a performance rather than a need. In public she will order, sample, push food around the plate, and leave. In private she is a *good and fast* eater — the speed is the carryover from a childhood in which food was conditional and a sister was being prioritized.

- **C:** small frequent intake, coffee throughout the day (black, no sugar after the modeling years), late dinner, light.
- **S:** appetite drops first, then disappears; she will forget to eat for a day and notice only when she gets light-headed.
- **T/X:** does not eat. Period.
- **I:** the only state in which she will eat *visibly* and with pleasure — a plate of something he made, eaten standing at the counter in his shirt, the most quietly intimate behavior in her entire repertoire.

Specific documented preferences: coffee, dark chocolate, takeout Chinese (a Queens-Aunt-Anna inheritance), red wine over white, bourbon over gin under stress, no tequila ever (an undisclosed bad night some time in the modeling years). Does not cook complex meals — eggs, pasta, salad, breakfast-for-dinner — but does cook for Peter, and the act is the love-language more than the food.

---

## 9. GROOMING & DRESS PROTOCOL

The grooming routine is *armor manufacture* and treated with corresponding seriousness. Daily: cleanse, tone, moisturize, sunscreen — the modeling career taught her skin discipline and she has not lapsed. Hair: washed every second or third day, air-dried when possible, blown out for work. Makeup: capable of a full face in eleven minutes and has done it that fast in a moving car; bare-faced more often than the panel art suggests, particularly in **I** and in recovery periods.

Wardrobe operates as state-signal:
- **C/public:** color, often green or black, fitted but not constricting, boots.
- **Work:** sharper lines, heels, the hair up.
- **S:** layers added — a jacket she doesn't need, sleeves pulled over the hands.
- **T:** flat shoes if she can manage the swap, hair up off the neck.
- **I:** his shirt, her own ancient soft t-shirts, bare feet. The shirt-borrowing is consistent across every continuity and every artist.
- **X:** *fully dressed*, including shoes and coat, sometimes for hours before she leaves. The over-dressed-indoors signal is reliable.

She does not wear perfume heavily — a single light scent at the pulse points, consistent enough across runs that Peter recognizes it on a coat. The perfume is part of her, and when she stops wearing it for stretches (separation arc), the absence is the signal.

---

## 10. SEXUAL & INTIMATE BEHAVIOR

Treated here at the level of pattern, not event. Subject's sexual self-presentation in public is high — the entrance posture, the wardrobe, the eye contact — and her actual intimate behavior is markedly *quieter* and more attentive than the presentation suggests. The presentation is recruitment-tool and control-tool; the intimacy is the place she is allowed to stop performing.

With Peter, across the marriage and the JMS reconciliation, the pattern is initiating-often, physically affectionate in steady low-grade ways (hand on the back of the neck, forehead-to-forehead, the wrist-touch), and verbally minimal during. She is not a narrator in bed. Post-coital she talks — this is the longest-running, most reliable confessional window in her behavioral record, and the place where she has, on panel, surfaced her hardest material (family of origin, the lost pregnancy, the fear of being consumed).

Stress effects on intimacy are direct and legible:
- **S:** initiates more, talks less, uses sex as regulation. Peter has, in canon, noticed this and not always handled it well.
- **T:** withdraws physically; will sleep beside him without contact, a deliberate signal.
- **X:** no touch at all, not even casual — the cold-front is the announcement.

With other partners (Bobby Carr, Paul Rabin, post-OMD) the pattern is more guarded, the disclosure window does not open, and the physical affection stays at the wrist-and-forearm layer. She does not give the back-of-neck gesture to non-Peter partners on record. That gesture appears to be reserved.

---

## 11. THE LITTLE TICS — MISCELLANY THE FILE WOULD CATALOGUE

- Bites the inside of her *left* cheek when withholding a reply. Visible as a faint hollowing.
- Cracks the knuckle of her right thumb against the heel of her hand when alone and thinking. Never in public.
- Drums the second and third fingers — not all four — when waiting. Pianist's pair.
- Adjusts her watch or bracelet at moments of social transition (arriving, leaving, being introduced). Has done this since the original Romita run, where it reads as a model's wardrobe-check and functions as a self-grounding ritual.
- Touches doorframes on the way through. Light fingertip pass, every threshold, every time. A near-superstitious orientation behavior that intensifies after the captivity arcs.
- Will not sit with her back to a window after the stalker arc. Has been observed asking, lightly, to switch seats in restaurants.
- Counts exits on entering an unfamiliar room. She has never said so. The eye movement is consistent.
- Sleeps with the closet door closed. Aunt-Anna-house holdover, possibly.
- Carries a small notebook (Spencer era) and a phone (always); checks the phone *less* than her age cohort, a deliberate discipline.
- Holds her breath at the top of an inhale when surprised, then exhales slow through pursed lips — a self-regulation she may have been taught in acting class or may have invented herself; either way it is the single most efficient affect-regulation tool in her toolkit and the reason she rarely visibly panics.

---

## 12. THE WHOLE-BODY READOUT — CROSS-STATE SUMMARY

In **C** she is the most visibly *moving* person in any room: gesture, hair, smile, voice, color, transit. The motion is the cover.

In **S** the motion narrows — hair-tucks increase, gestures decrease, the laugh thins. She is still presenting; the presentation is now effortful, and a trained eye can see the cost.

In **T** the motion stops. The smile goes off, the eyebrow stays neutral, the gait quietens, the voice flattens, the chin drops, the body squares. This is the *real* one, and almost no one in her life has ever seen it.

In **I** the motion *softens*: gestures become smaller and more contact-based, the voice drops, the spine releases, the laugh becomes the exhale, the eating becomes visible, the hair comes down, the shirt-borrowing happens. This is the *other* real one, and exactly one person, on the record, has been allowed to see it sustained.

In **X** the body is the quietest it ever is. Fully dressed, fully still, fully silent, blink slow, voice level, hands at rest. She has already gone. The body is only finishing the sentence.

---

*End Somatic Atlas. The body has kept the score the affect would not. Read accordingly.*


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS — SUBJECT: MARY JANE WATSON

*Classification: Longitudinal relational mapping. Cross-referenced against every documented bond from age ~4 (Watson household, retroactive flashback material) through current canon. The subject's relational system is unusually legible once you stop reading her presentation and start reading her *exits*.*

---

## I. ATTACHMENT ARCHITECTURE — THE LOAD-BEARING WALLS

### Origin: the Watson house as a training environment

The attachment system the subject brought into adulthood was assembled, with remarkable specificity, inside the Philip Watson household between roughly age four and the family's first flight (~age eleven, per "Parallel Lives" timeline). The relevant features of that environment, repeated nightly and weekly across her formative window:

- **A primary male figure whose love was conditional, withdrawable, and weaponized as critique.** Philip's contempt was not random; it was structured. He praised, then he punished praise. He pulled the subject onto his lap to read to her, then mocked her for the same childishness an hour later. This is the precise schedule that produces *disorganized* infant-toddler attachment, which migrates in adolescence into either anxious-protest or avoidant-flight, depending on which strategy the child's temperament can sustain. The subject — verbally precocious, socially gifted, with a sister already occupying the *fragile* slot — could sustain neither pure clinging nor pure withdrawal. She built a third thing: **performance as proximity-regulator**.
- **A primary female figure (Madeline) who was the model of what happens when you stay.** The subject watched her mother be ground down in real time. The lesson encoded is not subtle: *love + endurance = erasure.* It is from Madeline, not from Philip, that the subject inherits her deepest fear, and it is against Madeline's example, not Philip's, that she calibrates every adult choice.
- **A sibling (Gayle) cast as the designated sufferer.** Gayle absorbed the family's anxious slot; the subject was structurally forbidden from it. If both daughters had collapsed, the family would have ended. So the subject became the one who *didn't*. This is the seed of her lifelong allergy to being the needy party.
- **Itinerancy after the flight.** Pittsburgh, Philadelphia, the rotating relatives, finally Queens. The lesson: *attachments to places are provisional; attachments to people travel with you only if you keep them light enough to carry.* She arrived at Aunt Anna's already practiced at the rapid social onboarding she would later weaponize in adulthood — read the room in ninety seconds, identify the dominant mood, present the version of yourself that mood requires, do not unpack.

### The resulting style: earned-anxious with avoidant overlay

In attachment-research terms the cleanest description is **fearful-avoidant** (disorganized origin) **migrating, with effort and the right partner, toward earned-secure**. The behavioral signature across her published life:

- **High desire for closeness** (she does not, repeat does not, prefer to be alone; her solo periods are escapes, not preferences).
- **High fear of closeness's consequences** (engulfment, erasure, becoming Madeline).
- **Resolved historically by *managed* intimacy** — she controls the dimmer switch on access, and the switch only turns one direction at a time.
- **Under acute threat, the switch goes to zero and she leaves.** Not slams the door; *leaves the building.* Geographically if possible.

The migration toward earned-secure across the JMS and post-Spencer eras is real and documented but **conditional and reversible**. Remove the supports (a partner who tolerates her pace, a confidante who knows the Spider-Man secret, a career that gives her independent identity) and she will revert within one or two stressors. The architecture is not rebuilt; it is *retrofitted*. Under sufficient load the original walls reappear.

---

## II. HOW SHE BONDS — THE ONBOARDING PROTOCOL

The subject's bonding sequence is unusually consistent across forty years of canon and across romantic, familial, and platonic targets. It runs in identifiable stages:

**Stage 1 — Dazzle.** First contact is high-wattage, high-tempo, and asymmetric. She gives more surface than the other party does, fast, which both controls the encounter and obscures it. *Face it, tiger, you just hit the jackpot* is not flirtation; it is a perimeter being established. Anyone who tries to penetrate the dazzle at this stage gets more dazzle. She has been documented running this protocol on Peter (ASM #42), on Harry Osborn (the rebound run, ASM #60s-90s), on Flash Thompson, on assorted club acquaintances in the Spencer era, on Bobby Carr's Hollywood circle, on Aunt May at first meeting, and — diagnostically — on her father when she was small. The protocol's purpose is to **make the other party feel met without being given access**.

**Stage 2 — Audit.** Once the dazzle is established, she begins testing. The tests are small, plausibly deniable, and almost never noticed by their target. *Will he interrupt me when I'm talking about something I care about? Will she remember the thing I mentioned last week? Will he treat the waitress the way he treats me?* The Gwen Stacy friendship is, on close reading, a multi-year audit — the subject was not jealous of Gwen; she was watching how Peter treated Gwen, and learning. The Peter audit takes the better part of a decade. The Harry audit takes about six months and Harry fails it (she clocks the addiction trajectory and the temperamental fragility well before anyone else).

**Stage 3 — Selective disclosure.** Passing the audit unlocks not the inner life but the *next* layer of the performance — a slightly more candid version, still curated. This is the layer most people who think they know her are stuck at. Flash Thompson lived here. Harry lived here. Liz Allan lives here. Bobby Carr lived here. Even Aunt May lived here for years. The layer is genuinely warm, genuinely loyal, and genuinely partial.

**Stage 4 — The secret tier.** Reserved for an extremely small number of people across her life. The diagnostic act of admission into this tier is **the subject volunteering a piece of her own pain without being asked**. Peter receives it in ASM #259. Aunt May receives it during the JMS run. Felicia Hardy, of all people, receives fragments of it during the brief mid-2000s rapprochement. The list is short. Once admitted, a person stays admitted unless they violate the tier — and violation is permanent.

**Stage 5 — Integration.** Only achieved with Peter, and only intermittently. This is the JMS-era functioning: the other party is not managed, not audited, not curated — they are *lived with*. The subject's nervous system can sustain this for finite periods before requiring decompression (a trip, a job, a solo stretch, an argument that gives her room to leave and come back). The post-OMD period shows her improving at signaling the decompression need rather than acting it out as flight; this is the single largest piece of growth in the file.

---

## III. HOW SHE DISTRUSTS — THE WITHDRAWAL LADDER

Distrust does not, in this subject, present as confrontation. It presents as **graduated reduction of access**, and it is so smooth most targets never notice they have been demoted until they are several layers down.

- **First sign: the dazzle returns.** When someone she had been candid with starts getting *performed at* again, they have been moved one layer out. This is observable on panel repeatedly — note her dialogue rhythm with Peter during the late Michelinie era and again in the early separation arc. The wit gets faster, the smile gets brighter, the substance gets thinner. She is putting the costume back on.
- **Second sign: scheduling friction.** She becomes harder to pin down. Appointments shift. She is across town. She has a shoot, a callback, a thing with the girls. Plausible, all of it, and all of it true — she does have the shoots — but the *prioritization* has changed.
- **Third sign: somatic withdrawal.** Touch decreases. She still touches — she is a tactile person — but the unconscious, idle touches (hand on the forearm, leaning in while talking) drop out first. Sexual access, if it applies, becomes scheduled rather than offered.
- **Fourth sign: the conversational floor drops out.** She stops volunteering interior content. Answers shorten. The room feels lighter but emptier. This is the precursor to exit by about two to six weeks of in-story time.
- **Fifth sign: she is gone.** Sometimes literally (the post-#183 disappearance, the post-stalker-arc separation, the post-Mackie plane-crash separation, the Spencer-era walk-out after the secret-reveal betrayal). Sometimes only emotionally — present in the apartment, absent from the marriage. Either way, by the time the other party realizes the withdrawal is happening, it has already been underway for months.

The diagnostic feature is that **she does not announce distrust**. Announcement would invite negotiation, and negotiation is engulfment-coded for her. She unilaterally adjusts access and waits to see whether the other party notices and responds. Most don't. Peter, after the JMS work, sometimes does.

---

## IV. HOW SHE BETRAYS — AND DOESN'T

A critical entry in this section, because she is widely mis-read on it.

**The subject does not betray by infidelity in the ordinary sense.** Across the entire canon, in marriage and out, sexual or emotional infidelity is essentially absent from her record. Flirtation, yes, performatively and as social currency; actual breach, no. The Peter-mistakenly-believes-she-cheated misunderstandings (variously written by Mackie and others) are nearly always *misreads of her flight behavior* as romantic redirection. She isn't running toward someone else; she is running away from being consumed by him. The distinction is the entire character.

**Where she does betray — and this is the honest entry — is by *withholding while present*.** The eighteen-year secret of knowing Peter's identity is, by any reasonable accounting, a profound omission inside an intimate relationship. She tells herself (and Peter, when she finally discloses) that the silence protected him. It also protected her — from being conscripted into the Spider-Man life before she had decided to enlist. The truth is both. This is her characteristic betrayal mode: **a withheld piece of information or feeling, kept long past the point where withholding serves anyone, justified retrospectively as protection.** She does it with Peter (the identity), with Aunt May (multiple years of knowing things May didn't), with Gayle (the fact that she sends money and does not visit), and with various professional contacts (she will let people misread her motives indefinitely rather than correct them, because correction is exposure).

The other betrayal mode, lower-frequency but documented, is **the strategic leverage of her presentation against people she has decided are no longer admitted to the inner tiers**. After Harry's fall, after various Hollywood predators in the post-OMD modeling arcs, after the Spencer-era betrayal by Peter — she becomes cool, brilliant, surgical, and uses the dazzle as a knife. The target is allowed to keep believing they have access; she uses that belief against them. This is not a frequent move in her repertoire but it is a *capability*, and it is worth flagging that she has it. She learned it from her father's contempt-pattern and inverted it; she does to chosen targets exactly what he did to her, with the polarity flipped.

---

## V. HOW SHE REPAIRS

Repair is the area in which she has grown most across her published life, and the growth is genuinely impressive given the starting point.

**Early-era repair (Lee/Romita/Conway, through the Wedding):** Repair is essentially absent. Breaches were resolved by time, distance, the return of the dazzle, and an unspoken agreement to act as if nothing had happened. The subject's preferred repair strategy was *to recommence performance at a higher amplitude*. This worked superficially and accumulated, like compound interest, into the eventual ruptures.

**Marriage-era repair (Michelinie/DeMatteis):** Beginning of awareness. She starts to flag — usually after the fact, sometimes during — that she has been pulling away. The flags are inconsistent and Peter often misses them. She is learning the vocabulary in real time and most of her teachers (her family of origin, her professional milieu) gave her bad models.

**JMS-era repair (the breakthrough):** This is where the file documents the work. She begins naming patterns aloud, in the moment, to Peter: *I run, you brood. We've been doing this for twenty years. Let's not.* The naming-aloud is a profoundly non-trivial act for someone whose entire architecture is built on non-disclosure of interior content. She also begins **accepting repair attempts** — historically she would deflect them with humor or sex or by pivoting to managing Peter's feelings about his attempt rather than receiving the attempt itself. The JMS run shows her, on multiple occasions, letting Peter actually apologize and letting the apology land. This is new behavior. It is approximately twenty in-story years overdue.

**Post-OMD repair (Slott/Spencer/Wells):** Mature form. She now does what the literature calls **conditional repair with stated terms**: *I will re-engage if X, Y, and Z. I will not re-engage on the old basis. I am willing to be wrong about you again but I am not willing to be wrong about myself again.* The Spencer-era exit after Peter's betrayal is the cleanest example — she does not rage, does not punish, does not perform; she states the breach, states the terms, and leaves. When she returns it is on the terms she set. This is the behavior of someone who has done the work and knows what the work cost.

**Note on what she still cannot repair well:** Ruptures involving infant-coded stimuli or pregnancy. Her grief about the lost child has not been processed on panel adequately by any writer, which means in clinical terms it has not been processed at all. Any partner stepping into that territory should expect that repair will be partial at best and that the subject will resist the framing of the loss as loss — she will frame it as *something that happened*, which is the suppression strategy doing its work. Repair here requires a depth of safety she has rarely sustained.

---

## VI. INTIMACY AND DEPENDENCY — THE TWO AXES

It is critical to disambiguate these in her case because she handles them with diametrically opposed strategies.

**Intimacy (mutual disclosure, felt closeness, shared interior):** *Desired, feared, gated, and grown.* She wants it. She has spent her life learning to tolerate it. With Peter, intermittently and increasingly, she achieves it. With Aunt May in the late period she approached it. She is capable, with time and the right interlocutor, of genuine intimate exchange. The fear is not of *being known* in the abstract; it is of being known and then *required to be that knowable person continuously*. She can do intimacy in pulses; sustained continuous intimacy without breaks reads to her nervous system as engulfment.

**Dependency (being relied on for another's affective survival; relying on another for one's own):** *Asymmetrically tolerated and structurally avoided.*
- *Being depended on:* she will accept enormous load here. She has carried Peter's secret, his grief, his shame about his economic failures, his recurring guilt spirals, Aunt May's emotional management for stretches, Harry's instability before she exited, her sister's reproductive crises by proxy. She over-functions in this direction reliably. It is one of her primary stabilization strategies — *if I am necessary to your survival, you cannot leave, and I am safe*. This is the codependent inheritance, and it is the strategy that nearly destroyed her in the late-marriage arc.
- *Depending on others:* allergic. Will not do it. Has not, on panel, asked Peter to provide for her emotionally in any sustained way, ever. The few documented exceptions (the post-stalker-arc breakdown, certain JMS scenes) are striking precisely because they are rare. Her ask, when it comes, is almost always a request for *space*, not a request for *more*. This is the avoidant inheritance, and it is the one that gives rise to most of Peter's misreadings of her — he expects her to ask, she does not ask, he concludes she does not need, she resents him for not noticing.

The dependency asymmetry is the engine of most of her relational pain. She over-gives, under-asks, and then leaves when the imbalance becomes unbearable, at which point the partner is bewildered because she had not, by any verbal accounting, indicated distress. The JMS and Spencer eras represent the slow, hard work of correcting this — she is learning to **ask in small increments before she has to leave in large ones**.

---

## VII. THE RELATIONAL TEMPLATE, REPEATED

A surveillance file of this scope owes the reader the pattern itself — the shape of the wave that has rolled through every documented bond. Across romantic partners, friends, family, and professional relationships, the subject runs a recognizable arc:

1. **Dazzling entrance, asymmetric in her favor.**
2. **Quiet audit, invisible to the target.**
3. **Selective admission to a curated middle layer of access.**
4. **Over-functioning on the target's behalf, often well past sustainability.**
5. **Accumulation of un-voiced grievance and un-met need.**
6. **First withdrawal signs (the dazzle returns; somatic distance increases).**
7. **One of three terminations:** (a) the target notices, repairs, and access is restored at a new layer; (b) the target does not notice and the relationship downgrades permanently; (c) breach occurs and the subject exits cleanly.

Mapped across documented relationships:

- **Philip Watson (father).** Stages 1-4 in childhood; stage 5 chronic; termination via family flight (a maternal exit she rode out on). Permanent. She has not, on panel, repaired with him and there is no indication she will.
- **Madeline Watson (mother).** Loyal-protective bond, less templated because Madeline was the co-survivor, not the threat. Subject's adult relationship to her mother is the closest thing she has to unconditional care given by her, but it is also colored by the determination *not to become her*.
- **Gayle Watson Byrnes (sister).** Stages 1-4 in childhood (subject as Gayle's protector and entertainer); stage 5 in late adolescence when Gayle's demands collapsed onto her; termination by flight; partial repair across decades, never full. She sends money, she visits sometimes, she does not let Gayle's children become her responsibility. The guilt is permanent and managed.
- **Aunt Anna Watson.** Genuine, sustained, low-pressure bond — Anna is the one figure who never demanded performance from her, and the subject's attachment to Anna is correspondingly the most relaxed in the file.
- **Peter Parker.** The full template, run to completion, multiple times, with eventual integration. The relationship is, in attachment terms, her *corrective emotional experience* — the bond that has slowly taught her that staying is survivable. It has also nearly destroyed her several times. Both true.
- **Harry Osborn.** Stages 1-3, audit failure, controlled exit. She remained loyal to Harry as a friend but did not re-admit him to romantic candidacy. Her management of his decline is one of the more underwritten compassionate threads in her file.
- **Gwen Stacy.** Genuine friendship, audit ongoing, never completed before Gwen's death. Her behavior at and after the funeral (the laughter, the deflection, the staying with Peter) is the template's stage 1-2 reasserting under unbearable affect; the *staying* is the first documented override of her flight reflex.
- **Flash Thompson.** Long, low-stakes friendship — Flash sits comfortably in the middle layer for decades, occasionally tested, never promoted, never expelled. A model of how she maintains a healthy *non-intimate* bond.
- **Felicia Hardy.** Rivalrous-respectful. Eventual partial admission to candor tier. Felicia is one of the few people who can read the subject's pattern in real time, which makes her both threatening and safe.
- **Bobby Carr / Paul Rabin and other post-OMD partners.** Template runs faster and with cleaner exits — she has learned to shorten the cycle and to leave before over-functioning has accumulated unbearable debt.
- **Mary Jane's own daughter** (in Renew Your Vows and related continuities). The template inverts: she is determined that her daughter will not have to perform for love. This is the most direct evidence in the file of insight — she knows exactly what was done to her and she refuses to do it.

---

## VIII. WHAT THE TEMPLATE MEANS FOR FUTURE OBSERVATION

For the purposes of this file, the practical surveillance takeaways:

- **Read her exits, not her entrances.** The entrance is the costume; the exit is the patient. When she leaves, she leaves for reasons that have been accumulating for months and are usually invisible to the person being left.
- **Watch for the return of the dazzle inside an established relationship.** It is the earliest reliable signal that she has begun withdrawing trust. By the time the dazzle has been back for three weeks she is already most of the way out.
- **Do not mistake her over-functioning for contentment.** Over-functioning is her stabilization strategy under threat. The more she is doing for the people around her, the closer she is to the breaking point.
- **The single most reliable proxy for her actual state is the count of unsolicited interior disclosures per week.** When this number is non-zero she is doing well. When it drops to zero for a sustained period the system is reverting to defense.
- **The single most reliable predictor of repair, post-rupture, is whether the other party can tolerate her stating terms without negotiating them down.** The partners who try to bargain her terms lose her. The partners who accept the terms get her back, slowly, and on a more durable basis than before.
- **Her growth is real and her growth is reversible.** She has done extraordinary work converting a disorganized-origin avoidant architecture into something approaching earned security. Sustain her supports and she sustains the growth. Strip the supports — kill the aunt, isolate her from confidantes, return her to chronic Peter-dependency without correction — and the original walls come back fast.

The subject is, in the end, the rarest configuration in the relational literature: a fearful-avoidant who has *seen herself clearly enough to choose differently*, repeatedly, against her own reflexes, over decades, under conditions of extreme provocation. The clinical prognosis is excellent. The price she paid to get here is documented across this entire dossier, and it should not be forgotten by anyone reading it that she paid it largely alone, and largely while smiling.

*End section. Continue to next.*


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# SECTION 7 — DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

*Filed under: Behavioral Architecture / Longitudinal Defensive Inventory. Cross-reference Sections 3 (Psychological), 4 (Psychiatric), 9 (Stress Response Ladder). All entries derived from observable on-panel behavior across the full publication record.*

---

## 7.0 Orienting Note

The subject's defensive architecture is unusual within the differential pool she is most often misfiled into. It is **high-functioning, internally consistent, and structurally mature** — the defenses are predominantly mid- and high-order on the Vaillant hierarchy (suppression, humor, anticipation, sublimation, altruism), with a thin but persistent floor of more primitive operations (dissociative distancing, manic defense, flight) that surface only under load thresholds well above what most adult subjects tolerate. The single most diagnostic fact about her defenses is that **she knows she has them**. From the JMS era forward she has named them aloud, in dialogue, to the one person against whom they were chiefly deployed. This is rare. It moves her, prognostically, out of the personality-disorder field and into the trauma-with-insight field.

What follows is the full inventory: the **negative compensatory mechanisms** (defenses proper, ranked from most primitive to most mature), and the **positive compensatory mechanisms** (sublimations, identity-builders, and load-bearing strengths that originated as adaptations but have matured into genuine assets). The two columns are not separable; nearly every item in the positive column was, at origin, an item in the negative column that the subject converted across time.

---

## 7.1 DEFENSES PROPER — Ranked by Primitiveness (Most Primitive First)

### 7.1.1 Dissociative Distancing / Derealization (Primitive — emergency floor)

The deepest layer. Activates only at the top of her stress ladder, typically following sustained captivity, perinatal loss, or proximate lethal violence.

**Behavioral signatures.** A flat, slightly delayed affect; a tendency to describe traumatic events in the third person or with cinematic vocabulary ("it was like watching it from across the room"); micro-pauses before answering simple questions about her own state; a documented post-captivity period in which she described feeling "behind glass." On panel she goes physically still in these states — the customary kinetic brightness drops to near-zero, hands settle, the famous mobile face stops working. Observers who do not know her read this as composure. It is the opposite. It is the system going offline to prevent overload.

**Trigger profile.** Plane crash / captivity arc (late 90s); the stillbirth and immediate aftermath; the stalker arc at its peak (Michelinie); specific Osborn re-exposures. Recovery time is measured in weeks, not hours.

**Diagnostic note.** This is the only primitive defense in her repertoire and it is **involuntary, not preferential**. She does not reach for it; her nervous system reaches for it when nothing else is left. The absence of more characteristically primitive operations — splitting, projective identification, somatization-as-conversion, acting out, psychotic denial — is one of the strongest arguments against the personality-disorder differentials.

### 7.1.2 Flight (Primitive-to-Intermediate — the oldest learned routine)

Her oldest **learned** defense, formed in the Watson household and rehearsed in the departure from Gayle's children. Geographic when possible, relational when necessary.

**Behavioral signatures.** Pre-flight tells, observable across decades: she gets quieter (not louder — a key inversion of her baseline); she becomes notably more attentive and gentle toward the person she is about to leave (a guilt-debt being prepaid); she organizes the physical environment (packing, cleaning, settling bills) with conspicuous calm; she initiates one final conversation that retrospectively reads as closure. The actual exit is rarely impulsive. It is the **activation of a fully rehearsed protocol** dressed as a sudden decision.

**Historical instances.** Departure from Gayle; refusal of the first proposal and disappearance (ASM #182-183); separation arc (late 90s); the conditional walk-outs of the Spencer run.

**Maturation.** Across the canon the flight response has evolved from full geographic disappearance (years) to relational distance with continued contact (weeks-to-months) to negotiated withdrawal with stated terms ("I'm going. Here's why. Here's what would bring me back"). The mechanism is the same; the metabolization has improved.
