- **Permission to leave without freight.** The sentence "I'll be here if you come back, and I'll be here if you don't" is the single most regulating thing anyone has ever said to her on the page (JMS, in substance, multiple times). It removes the only thing she cannot tolerate, which is being held in place.
- **Aunt May–coded presence**: an older woman, unhurried, doing something domestic in the same room. The subject's nervous system has decades of evidence that this configuration is safe.
- **Peter, when he is not himself in crisis.** His baseline is one of the only baselines she trusts. When he is steady, she can borrow it. When he is not, she cannot, and the calming function inverts.

**Somatic tells that the down-regulation is working.** The jaw unclenches first (she carries tension there; DeMatteis-era panels show it). Then the shoulders drop. Then she will make a small joke — almost always self-directed, almost always slightly bitter. The joke is the *all-clear*; before the joke, she is still managing.

---

## 3. THE PERSUASION VECTORS — HOW TO MOVE HER POSITION

She is not persuaded by argument. She is persuaded by *evidence accumulated over time* and by *trust in the source*. There is no single conversation that changes her mind on anything that matters; there are only conversations that add data points to a model she is running quietly.

**The high-bandwidth channel.** Show, do not tell. She updates beliefs about people from their behavior under pressure, and almost never from their stated intentions. The fastest way to move her position on whether someone is trustworthy is to let her watch them do something costly and consistent for someone who is not her, when they don't know she's watching.

**The receipts mechanism.** She remembers — in unsettling detail — what people have said and done. Anyone trying to persuade her of a new position has to first reconcile it with the back-catalogue of their own statements, which she has filed. Inconsistency does not enrage her; it quietly closes the channel. The persuader who openly acknowledges the contradiction ("I know I said the opposite three years ago; here's what changed") keeps the channel open. The one who pretends the contradiction isn't there loses her permanently and without notice.

**The loyalty-frame.** Arguments that bear on protection of people she has chosen route through a high-bandwidth channel; arguments that bear on her own self-interest route through a low-bandwidth, suspicious channel. To persuade her to do something *for herself*, frame it in terms of its effect on her chosen intimates; she will accept on their behalf what she will not accept on her own. (This is itself a vulnerability — it is the mechanism by which she has historically self-erased — but it is also a true lever.)

**What she will not be moved by.** Appeals to convention, to what is normally done, to what people will think. The subject has lived her entire adult life as a tabloid object and has built a calloused indifference to public opinion that is one of her stable strengths. Anyone trying to leverage social shame is wasting the bid.

---

## 4. THE PROVOCATION VECTORS — HOW TO GET A REACTION SHE DID NOT INTEND TO GIVE

These are the specific stimuli that bypass her control apparatus. They are documented because anyone with hostile intent will find them eventually; better that her people find them first.

**The Philip Watson register.** Intellectual condescension toward her, delivered with the specific flavor of *I am the serious one and you are the ornament*, will produce a reaction sequence: a half-second of stillness, then a smile that does not reach the eyes, then a verbal cut precisely calibrated to the speaker's known insecurity. She does not forget the speaker. The cut is the only externally visible part; the registration is permanent. This is the one provocation that overrides her usual policy of letting hostile parties believe they have won.

**The "frivolous" word and its cognates.** Any framing of her work, her career, or her concerns as decorative, lightweight, or unserious — particularly from a man, particularly from a man she has been generous to — produces cold, surgical, lasting withdrawal. She will not announce the withdrawal. The speaker will discover, weeks later, that he is no longer in her life.

**Being made responsible without consent.** "I need you" said in the engulfing register (as distinct from a specific request, which she handles capably) triggers the Gayle protocol. The first time, she absorbs it. The second time, she begins planning a route. The third time, she is already gone — she will simply have stopped being where the speaker expects her to be.

**Infant-coded stimuli under stress.** A baby crying in a context she cannot leave (a stalled subway car, a long flight, a hospital waiting room) will produce a specific dissociative withdrawal: she will go very still, her breathing will shallow, and she will not speak for some minutes. This is not controllable by her and she is not aware of how visible it is. People in her life should know to give her an exit at the first audible cry, without comment.

**Osborn-coded stimuli.** The name, the laugh, the color green deployed with the specific glossy lacquered quality, the pumpkin motif, anything that triggers the memory of the bridge or of the lost pregnancy. Her response is to go operational — she becomes very calm, very precise, very capable, and entirely inaccessible. This is the one threat she has trained herself against; the cost is that she cannot feel anything else while the Osborn channel is active.

**Performance of her own image back at her.** A person doing a knowing impression of her public persona, especially in flirtation, lands as an attack on the costume she has earned. The reaction is contempt, well-managed but unmistakable. Do not perform her at her.

**Being thanked for her loyalty.** Sincere acknowledgment of the secret-keeping, the years of management, the work she has done that no one is supposed to see — this is a *provocation* in the sense of producing involuntary affect. She will cry. She will hate having cried. The provocateur, if benign, must then not make it worse by commenting on it.

---

## 5. THE PREDICTION VECTORS — WHAT SHE WILL DO IN A GIVEN SITUATION

The subject's behavior is highly predictable to anyone who has correctly modeled the architecture. The following are forward-projections at high confidence.

**Under sudden bad news about Peter.** She will not panic visibly. She will ask one or two extremely precise questions, get up, do something logistical (call Aunt May, get to a location, find a screen), and only later — alone, hours later — process the affective load. If the bad news arrives in public, she will finish the social engagement first. The dissociative competence here is one of her most reliable behaviors.

**Under a marriage-stress arc.** The escalation ladder is invariant: humor up, then managing-of-Peter up, then somatic symptoms (insomnia, appetite loss), then secret-keeping intensifies, then a stretch of productive busyness that everyone around her mistakes for being fine, then — without warning to anyone but with weeks of internal warning to herself — exit. The exit will be framed as temporary and may be. The interval between "fine" and "gone" is shorter than observers think and longer than she thinks.

**Under a new romantic bid from outside the marriage.** Refusal, but graceful. She does not enjoy hurting the suitor and will provide them an exit that preserves their dignity. The exception is bids that come with the Philip-register condescension or the engulfing-need register; those receive the cold cut. She has not, on the record, been moved by any outside suitor whose offer was *more excitement*; she has been intermittently moved by offers of *more calm*, which is the channel that should worry the people who love her marriage.

**Under a professional setback.** Brief flattening, then strategic redirection. She has no ego investment in any specific career outcome (acting, modeling, nightclub ownership, etc.) — the ego investment is in *having a domain that is hers*, and the specific domain is fungible. She will pivot inside a week.

**Under a direct threat to Aunt May.** Operational mode. No hesitation, no negotiation, willingness to accept personal risk that she would not accept on her own behalf.

**Under a direct threat to herself.** Surprisingly calm. She has been kidnapped enough times to have a working protocol: keep the captor talking, keep the affect light, look for the exit, do not let them see fear because fear escalates them. The protocol is conscious. It will hold for hours.

**When complimented sincerely on something other than her appearance.** Brief surprise, brief warmth, then a deflection that returns the compliment to the speaker. She does not know how to receive these. This is itself a vulnerability — a person who can deliver such compliments steadily and without expectation of return acquires bandwidth with her that no other channel provides.

---

## 6. THE DESTABILIZATION VECTORS — HOW HER ARCHITECTURE FAILS

Documented for protection. These are the conditions under which her unusually robust regulation system breaks.

**Compounded load over time without a witness.** She can carry enormous weight if one trusted person knows she is carrying it. She cannot carry medium weight in total isolation indefinitely. The 1990s stalker arc and the late-90s separation arc both show the same mechanism: a stressor she could not name to Peter (because naming it would burden him in a way she would not permit) accumulated past the metabolizable threshold and produced collapse. The destabilizer, malign or otherwise, is *isolation in the presence of stress*. The protective inverse is a confidant who is not Peter — historically Aunt May, sometimes Felicia Hardy in odd configurations, occasionally Carlie Cooper in the post-OMD era — to whom she can offload without the engulfment alarm.

**Removal of her exits.** She is calm in proportion to her sense that she could, if she chose, leave. Closing exits — relational, geographic, financial — produces escalating distress that culminates in her taking the exit she previously had no intention of taking. The lesson, learned by Peter and forgotten by him on cycles: the open door is what keeps her in the room.

**Engulfing need delivered by a person she loves.** The single most reliable destabilizer in her file. Not anger, not betrayal, not threat — *need*, delivered with the implicit message that her continued presence is the speaker's life-support. The Gayle template loads here and she goes into flight-prep within hours.

**Sleep deprivation.** Her defenses are metabolically expensive. Three nights of poor sleep and the humor-deflection apparatus degrades visibly; four nights and the dissociative distancing arrives. The pattern is documented across the stalker arc and the captivity-aftermath arc. People who love her should treat her sleep as load-bearing infrastructure.

**Alcohol past two drinks in a high-affect context.** Suppression requires executive function; alcohol degrades it; she becomes either flat or, more dangerously, honest. The honesty is not pleasant for her the next day. The protective party orders her food.

**The specific combination of perinatal-loss reactivation and Osborn-coded stimuli.** This combination has not been deployed in canon at full intensity since the Clone Saga and the immediate aftermath. If deployed, predicted response is severe and possibly beyond her current coping repertoire. Flag as a category-of-one vulnerability.

**Public revelation of Peter's identity by a third party.** Strips her of the one act of agency she has performed continuously since adolescence — the choice to know and to hold. Predicted response: not anger at the revealer (she will compartmentalize that), but a profound and possibly extended period of derealization, because the structure that has organized her adult life has been altered without her consent.

---

## 7. THE PROTECTIVE COUNTER-LEVERAGE — WHAT KEEPS HER WHOLE

Cataloged so that the people around her know what to maintain.

**A confidant who is not Peter.** Non-negotiable infrastructure. The category matters more than the specific identity; what is required is one person who knows the full weight, who does not require her to manage them in return, and who will not relay to Peter.

**Work that is hers.** Any domain — creative, commercial, social — over which she has unilateral authority and from which her identity draws independent income. Take this away and the marriage-frame becomes load-bearing in a way it cannot sustainably bear.

**Physical movement.** She regulates through her body. A long walk, a dance floor, a swim, a stage rehearsal — kinetic activity discharges the load that suppression has accumulated. Sedentary stress periods are when she breaks.

**Aunt May, while available.** The single most stabilizing presence in her ecosystem, for reasons that go beyond Peter. May is the only adult who has ever consistently treated her as a person without an agenda. The loss of May, when it comes, will require active replacement of that function or the regulation system will degrade.

**Peter's steadiness, when he can offer it.** Reciprocal: she stabilizes against his baseline, and his baseline stabilizes against hers. The marriage works when both regulators are online; it fails when both are offline simultaneously. The protective inference is that they should not be in acute crisis at the same time, and that the one with more current capacity should hold the floor for the other, deliberately and explicitly.

**Her own named language for her patterns.** The JMS-era articulations — *I run, you brood* and its variants — are not throwaway lines. They are the active ingredient in her current functioning. Anyone who helps her keep that language alive (by using it back to her, by not letting her drop it under stress) is contributing to her stability.

**Exits she does not have to take.** The knowledge that she can leave is sufficient; she does not require leaving. Preserve the option visibly and the option will go unused.

---

## 8. THE META-VULNERABILITY

The single most dangerous fact in this compendium is that the subject has constructed her own protections with such skill that the people around her, including those who love her, routinely underestimate how much weight she is carrying at any given moment. She presents calm and competent until approximately ninety seconds before she presents gone. The protective lesson is: *do not wait for the signal*. There will not be one. Build the supports, maintain the confidant, preserve the exits, witness the load that she will not name, and the architecture holds. Let any of these slip on the assumption that she will tell you when it matters, and she will not tell you, and one morning the apartment will be empty and the note will be on the counter and the handwriting will be steady.

She has trained for the exit since she was nine years old. It is the most practiced behavior in her file.

The work of the people who love her is to make sure she never has to use it.

— END SECTION —


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# DOSSIER SECTION 5 — STRENGTHS, ASSETS & RESILIENCE

*Subject: Watson, Mary Jane. The positive ledger. What she has, what she does well, what has kept her standing across sixty years of published incident and what will keep her standing through the next sixty. Read this section against Section 3 (Psychological) and Section 4 (Psychiatric) — most of her strengths are the dorsal side of the same vertebrae her wounds run along; the file would be inaccurate to either if it failed to itemize both.*

---

## 5.1 COGNITIVE & PERCEPTUAL ASSETS

**Social cognition at the high end of the human range.** The single most underrated capability on the ledger. Subject reads rooms with a speed and accuracy that, in a different developmental context, would have made her a competent intelligence officer or trial litigator. The diagnostic instance is the secret-identity catch — adolescent, no priors, single behavioral observation outside Aunt May's house the night Ben Parker was killed, and the inference held under nearly two decades of in-story confirmation pressure without leaking once. That is not luck. That is a pattern-recognition engine trained from age four upward on a volatile household where misreading the room had physical consequences. She runs the same engine on every subsequent room.

**Predictive emotional modeling.** She forecasts other people's affective weather two and three moves out. In observed behavior this looks like: arriving at gatherings already knowing who will pair off, who will leave early, who needs to be steered away from whom; pre-empting Peter's spirals before he has consciously begun them; managing Aunt May's news-intake with surgical timing. The operational value of this faculty in a household partnered to a costumed combatant cannot be overstated — she is, functionally, his emotional radar net.

**Crisis-state clarification.** Under acute threat her cognition does not narrow into panic; it widens and *clarifies*. Hostage records (Hobgoblin, Chameleon, Mysterio, Osborn) consistently show her negotiating, stalling, gathering intelligence, and conserving her captor's tolerance for her continued existence. She has talked her way out of more rooms than her file's "civilian" classification would predict. The mechanism is the same engine — under stress she reads faster, not slower.

**Verbal facility.** High. Subject's vocabulary, register-shifting, and improvisational fluency are documented across decades. She code-switches between go-go-club argot, theater-people industry vocabulary, fashion-industry register, Forest Hills domestic register, and tabloid-evasion register without seams. This is the working tool of both her professional careers and her social camouflage.

**Memory profile.** Strong episodic memory for relational data, weaker for impersonal abstraction (no canonical academic record of note). She remembers who said what to whom and when, and she stores grievances accurately without necessarily acting on them — a *librarian* memory for the social field, which makes her difficult to deceive twice.

---

## 5.2 PERFORMATIVE & PROFESSIONAL ASSETS

**Trained acting capability.** Not amateur. Subject worked stage and television through the late 70s and 80s, carried a daytime serial role, and has periodically returned to the craft across the JMS and post-OMD eras. The asset has three dimensions worth itemizing:

1. *Technical craft* — voice control, body control, the ability to land a take on cue. These are real, transferable skills with cash value and identity value.
2. *Affective distance through character* — the acting work doubles as the highest-functioning version of her primary defense (intellectualization-through-performance, Section 3). She metabolizes her own feelings by lending them to roles. This is healthier than it sounds; it is a sublimation channel of unusually high bandwidth.
3. *Reading other actors* — sharpens her already-elite social cognition; the craft trained her to watch micro-expressions professionally.

**Modeling career.** Long, lucrative, longitudinal. The asset is not the face — the face is a fact of biology and a complication as often as it is a tool. The asset is that she *worked the business*: managed agents, navigated photographers, knew which jobs to take and which to refuse, understood her market and aged through it with strategic intelligence rather than denial. This is small-business operator behavior dressed as glamour work.

**Business ownership / management.** Documented across post-OMD canon as nightclub owner and operator. The skill set on display — staffing, vendor management, regulatory navigation, security coordination, cash-handling discipline, the social engineering of an after-hours venue — is the most underrated professional asset in the file. A woman who can keep a profitable Manhattan club running clean is a woman with executive capacity.

**Earnings history and financial independence.** She has, at multiple points in her published life, out-earned Peter Parker by an order of magnitude. The relevance to the asset ledger is not the money per se but what the money *means*: she has never been economically captive to the relationship. Her exits have always been live options, which is what has allowed her stays to be authentic.

---

## 5.3 INTERPERSONAL & ATTACHMENT ASSETS

**Loyalty as load-bearing virtue.** Subject's loyalty is not sentimental — it is *infrastructural*. Once she has selected someone (Peter, May, Anna Watson, later Annie in alternates), the commitment functions as a hard structural element of her life around which other decisions arrange themselves. The eighteen-year unilateral secret-keeping is the proof-of-load: she carried operational weight for a person who did not know she was carrying it, with no reward and considerable cost, because she had decided to. Loyalty of that quality is rare and is the bedrock asset of the entire file.

**Capacity for repair.** Demonstrated across the JMS reconciliation and again across the Spencer-era re-engagements. Subject can: (a) name a relational rupture aloud; (b) tolerate the other party's defensive response without escalating; (c) propose specific behavioral changes; (d) hold the other party to them without becoming punitive. This skill set is uncommon in clinical populations and was *self-acquired* — there is no canonical therapist in her history. She built it.

**Warmth at the surface, durably.** Whatever the underlying architecture, the warmth she presents to strangers, children, and acquaintances is not performance in the cynical sense — it is real social generosity, deployed reliably, and people consistently report feeling better for having been near her. This is a community asset; she is a net contributor to whatever room she enters.

**Caretaking capacity, calibrated.** Section 3 catalogues caretaking-as-control as a lower-grade negative; in the asset column it is also a real strength. She is genuinely good at tending to people in distress — practical (food, logistics, rides, calls), emotional (presence without crowding), informational (knows what to say and what to withhold). Aunt May's late-life depictions are full of subject quietly handling things May would otherwise have had to.

**Selective-trust calibration.** She does not trust easily, and once she does trust, she is slow to unrevoke even under provocation. Both halves of that are assets — the slow grant prevents catastrophic misallocation; the slow revocation prevents the splitting and churn that destabilize less-organized intimates.

---

## 5.4 SOMATIC & PHYSICAL ASSETS

**General health, robust.** No chronic illness on record. Cardiovascular and musculoskeletal baselines consistent with a person who has done modeling-required fitness work for decades — pilates, yoga, dance conditioning carried over from the go-go-era. She is not enhanced and not trained for combat, but she is conditioned, mobile, and durable.

**Stamina under sleep deprivation.** Documented across multiple arcs (Clone Saga, separation arc, repeated kidnapping recoveries). She functions on short sleep for extended periods without cognitive collapse — partially a learned skill from the modeling/acting schedule, partially a stress-trait from a household that did not reliably sleep.

**Beauty as instrument (with caveats).** The file would be dishonest not to list it. Subject's appearance is a documented social and professional instrument that has opened doors, deflected hostility, and bought time in negotiations. The caveats in Section 3 about it being isolating and pre-empting deeper knowability remain true. But as an instrument she has learned to wield it deliberately rather than be wielded by it, which is the form in which it becomes an asset rather than a liability.

**Pain tolerance.** Above population norm. Multiple captivity recoveries with no documented opiate dependence, no chronic-pain spiral, no somatization escalation. She metabolizes physical insult and moves on.

---

## 5.5 PSYCHOLOGICAL RESILIENCE FACTORS

**Absence of decompensation into the dangerous categories.** Despite a cumulative trauma load that would justify almost any psychiatric outcome, subject has never, on record: attempted suicide, self-harmed, decompensated into psychosis, developed a substance-use disorder, become incapacitated by depressive episode, or expressed her distress as violence toward others. The negative space in her psychiatric record is itself an asset of enormous magnitude. Many comparably-exposed adults are dead, hospitalized, or unrecognizable. She is none of these.

**Suppression as a high-order defense.** Section 3 flags suppression (conscious deferral of feeling) versus repression (unconscious exile of feeling). The former is, in the defense literature, one of the *mature* defenses — alongside humor, sublimation, and altruism, all of which she also deploys. Her defensive architecture, considered as a whole, is mature-skewing despite its developmental origin in a disorganized environment. This is the actuarially good news about her prognosis.

**Humor as connection-tool, not just deflection.** Distinguish from manic defense (Section 3, also real). The non-defensive humor — the dry, observational, often self-deprecating voice that emerges in low-threat intimate settings — is a genuine connection skill and a regulator of her own affect. It costs her nothing and earns her affiliation reliably.

**Sublimation channels in good working order.** Acting, modeling, business, parenting (in continuities where applicable), nesting/home-making, friendship. She has multiple legitimate outlets through which difficult affect can be metabolized into productive output. People with one channel are brittle; she has six.

**Insight, late-acquired but real.** The JMS-era line — *I run, you brood* — is the single most important marker of insight in the file. Subject can name her own pattern, name her partner's, and treat both as joint operational problems rather than character verdicts. Insight at this level is the prerequisite for change, and she has demonstrated the change as well as the insight.

**Capacity to walk away cleanly.** The Spencer-era exit after betrayal is exemplary. No scenes, no protracted negotiation, no return-and-rage cycle. The behavior catalogues as a negative in attachment terms (avoidant exit) and as a positive in life-management terms (she will not stay in a structurally unsafe configuration). Both readings are true; the positive should not be erased by the negative.

**No identity collapse under name/role pressure.** "Mrs. Parker," "model," "actress," "club owner," "ex-fiancée," "ex-wife," "the redhead" — the subject has been called all of these and has not been consumed by any of them. Her sense-of-self is built on something more durable than role.

---

## 5.6 SECURITY-RELEVANT CAPABILITIES (the spouse-of-a-target file)

**Operational discretion.** Eighteen years of perfect secret-keeping under conditions where leaks would have been ruinous. Subject is, by demonstrated track record, a Tier-1 confidant. The intelligence value of a person who can keep that magnitude of secret that long is hard to overstate.

**Counter-surveillance instincts, learned.** Years adjacent to a costumed combatant have trained subject in tail-detection, safe-routing, public-comms hygiene, decoy behavior, and threat-triage. She is not a tradecraft professional but she is a competent civilian operator and would calibrate fast under instruction.

**Hostage-survival aptitude.** Empirically demonstrated across many incidents. Subject does not panic, does not provoke, does not collapse; she negotiates time, conserves captor patience, and stays alert for extraction windows. She has been the hostage who *helped* the rescue more than once.

**Threat-assessment accuracy.** Reads bad rooms early. The stalker arc shows the failure mode (she clocked the threat and was still overwhelmed), but the read itself was correct and early — the failure was downstream of the read, in the resources available to her, not in the perception.

**Press management.** Subject has handled tabloid and gossip-press pressure for decades without major self-inflicted damage. The skill — what to say, what to withhold, when to feed a story to bury another — is a real and rare asset and is directly transferable to managing the public-facing aspects of any sensitive household.

---

## 5.7 SOCIAL CAPITAL & EXTERNAL RESOURCES

**Network breadth.** Subject's address book spans theater, fashion, hospitality, journalism, Forest Hills domestic, and superhero-adjacent (Avengers spouses, Fantastic Four social orbit). Few civilians in the file system have her density of cross-domain weak ties.

**Network depth.** Smaller but high-quality: Peter; May; Anna Watson (deceased / depending on continuity); Harry Osborn (complicated, intermittent); Felicia Hardy (rivalrous-respectful, occasionally collaborative); selected acting/modeling industry intimates of long duration. The depth tier is short but each entry is load-bearing.

**Reputational capital.** Across the published record, subject is consistently described by acquaintances as *kind*, *fun*, *generous*, *unflappable*. The reputation is itself an asset — it produces benefit-of-the-doubt in negotiations, employability, and social-emergency response.

**Geographic competence.** Multi-city. Pittsburgh, Philadelphia, Queens, Manhattan, Los Angeles, Chicago (Bobby Carr era). She can land in an unfamiliar metro and be functional within forty-eight hours — a skill carried over from the itinerant childhood and refined by professional travel.

**Domain literacy in entertainment industry.** Knows agents, knows contracts at a working level, knows the local power-brokers in two coastal entertainment ecosystems. This is liquid capital that converts to income on demand.

---

## 5.8 LONGITUDINAL / DEVELOPMENTAL ASSETS

**Trajectory direction is positive.** The most important sentence in this section. Across sixty years of canon, the *direction of travel* of subject's psychological functioning is upward — from go-go-era manic defense, through marriage-era over-functioning, through post-OMD calibrated independence, through JMS-era insight, through Spencer-era boundaried re-engagement. The slope is not monotonic (the Mackie separation arc, OMD-adjacent regressions) but the trendline is unmistakable. Most adults' trendlines flatten in the fourth decade. Hers is still rising.

**Self-directed change.** The change has not been imposed — no therapist of record, no inpatient intervention, no chemical management. She has been her own clinician. The therapeutic alliance she runs is with herself, and it has been productive. This is rare and prognostically excellent.

**Earned-security trajectory.** Attachment researchers reserve the category *earned-secure* for people who started insecure and worked their way to secure functioning through reflection and corrective experience. Subject is the textbook case. The earned-secure category, longitudinally, shows the best outcomes on most measures of life satisfaction, parenting capacity, and partner functioning of any attachment category — including continuously-secure. Subject has done the harder version of the work and is reaping its benefits.

**Resistance to writer-projection.** Across decades of being written by men who have variously attempted to make her shallow, manipulative, weak, saintly, or simply absent, the core architecture has re-asserted itself every time a writer attended to the canon. This is a comment about the character's robustness as a literary entity, but it functions in this file as a comment about the *recognizability* of her core — she is, across continuities and authorial intents, the same person. Identity stability of that quality is itself a resilience factor.

---

## 5.9 SUMMARY ASSET FORMULATION

Subject brings to any situation an unusual combination: an elite social-cognitive engine, mature defensive architecture, multiple working sublimation channels, an extensive and cross-domain network, professional skills with cash value across at least three industries, demonstrated operational discretion, hostage-survival aptitude, financial independence, robust general health, an upward-sloping psychological trajectory, and a self-built capacity for relational repair. She is loyal to a small number of people without limit, generous to a larger number without strain, and functionally competent in environments — domestic, professional, criminal-adjacent, and life-threatening — that would incapacitate most civilians of comparable training.

The shorthand the file should use, when shorthand is required: *she is the person you want in the room when the room goes bad, and she is the person who will still be standing in it after most of the others have left.* The wound that produced her is real and catalogued elsewhere in this dossier. The instrument the wound produced — and that she has, over six decades, sharpened, calibrated, and made her own — is one of the most resilient civilian profiles in the system.

End Section 5. Continue to Section 6 (Vulnerabilities, Pressure Points, & Failure Modes) for the inverse ledger.


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# FAILURE MODES & DECOMPENSATION — SUBJECT: MARY JANE WATSON

*Filed under: Behavioral Collapse Architecture. Cross-reference: §3 Psychological, §4 Psychiatric, §1 History (Gayle collapse; ASM #122; ASM #182-183; Clone Saga stillbirth; Mackie separation arc; Spencer betrayal arc).*

---

## 1. THE GOVERNING PRINCIPLE OF HER COLLAPSE

Before cataloguing the failure modes, the file must state the single fact that organizes all of them: **this subject does not break the way most people break.** The default human collapse vectors — rage outbursts, depressive shutdown, suicidal ideation, psychotic decompensation, self-harm, public scene-making — are largely absent from her record across sixty publication years and an in-universe trauma load that would flatten most documented combat veterans. She is not absent of these vectors because she is healthy; she is absent of them because her developmental environment selected, very early, for a *single* survival routine and refined it ruthlessly.

That routine is **exit**.

Every failure mode below is a variation on, or a precursor to, the activation of that routine. The escalation ladder is not a path toward explosion; it is a path toward *vanishing*. The Watcher trap with this subject is to look for the loud collapse and conclude, when no loud collapse appears, that she is fine. The loud collapse will not come. What comes instead is a sequence of progressively quieter accommodations until, at the terminal stage, she is no longer in the room — sometimes geographically, sometimes only behind glass behind her own eyes.

This must be understood: **her collapse is silent, productive-looking, and reversible only by being noticed early.**

---

## 2. THE ESCALATION LADDER — STAGES OF DECOMPENSATION

Six stages, with characteristic behavioral, somatic, and interpersonal signatures. The early stages are *load-bearing*; she can hold there for months. The late stages move quickly.

### Stage 1 — Compensatory Brightening (the "manic-defense up-shift")

Trigger: any introduction of stress, however minor. A bad audition. Peter forty minutes late. A news alert involving Osborn. A letter from Gayle.

Presentation:
- **Affect up.** Smile bigger, faster. Laugh at her own setup lines.
- **Verbal output up.** Sentence rate increases ~20–30%. More slang, more endearments ("tiger," "honey," "champ"), more nicknames deployed defensively as social lubricant.
- **Physical animation up.** Hands more active. More physical contact with whoever she is talking to — touching a forearm, fixing a collar, smoothing a shirt. This is not flirtation. It is *grounding behavior*, the somatic equivalent of holding her own elbows.
- **Wardrobe.** Subtle escalation toward color and visibility. She has been observed to dress *up* before a difficult conversation, never down. The performance armor is suited up before the engagement.
- **Selective topical avoidance** — she will steer conversation away from the triggering content with such graceful misdirection that the redirect itself is often the only diagnostic sign. Listen for what she *doesn't* allow into the room.

Duration: indefinite. She can sustain Stage 1 across years if the underlying stressor is chronic but low-amplitude. The entire 1966–1978 publication era is, in retrospect, an extended Stage 1.

Reversibility: trivially reversible. A single honest question from a trusted intimate, framed without demand, drops her out. *Reversibility collapses sharply at later stages.*

### Stage 2 — Managerial Over-Function

Trigger: stressor sustained past her tolerance for pure performance, or stressor specifically involving another person whose distress she has decided to absorb.

Presentation:
- **Caretaking escalation.** She begins running other people's logistics — meals, schedules, emotional weather reports. Aunt May's medication. Peter's photo deadlines. A friend's apartment hunt. The activity is real and competent, *and* it is a regulatory mechanism: managing others lets her postpone managing herself.
- **Domestic mobilization.** The apartment becomes cleaner. Cooking increases. She develops *projects* — repainting, reorganizing, redecorating. (J.M. DeMatteis run is rich with this.)
- **Calendar densification.** She accepts more work, more social engagements, more obligations. The schedule becomes the wall she puts between herself and her own interior.
- **Sleep onset begins to slip.** First somatic marker. She is the last one awake in the apartment, "just finishing one thing." Documented across the stalker arc.
- **Tobacco re-recruits.** Single cigarettes, on the fire escape, not in front of Peter. The relapse vector is reliable enough to be a forward indicator.
- **Mirror time increases** — not vanity, *self-checking*. She is verifying the costume is still on.

Duration: weeks to months.

Reversibility: still reversible, but requires more than a question — requires *insistence* by a trusted intimate, and the offering of relief from at least one of the managed responsibilities. Aunt May learning the secret in the JMS run is the structural example: when one of her loads was removed, she stepped down a stage within days.

### Stage 3 — Affective Constriction with Somatic Translation

Trigger: stressors at Stage 2 not resolved, or the entry of a stressor that touches a primary wound (Gayle-pattern obligation; engulfment-coded behavior from Peter; infant-coded stimuli; intellectual condescension echoing her father).

Presentation:
- **Affect band narrows.** Smile still present, but eyes disengage. Laugh becomes a beat late. The brightness goes from incandescent to fluorescent — same wattage, wrong spectrum. Anyone who has known her at Stage 1 will register the difference; strangers will not.
- **Verbal output flattens.** Sentences shorten. She becomes a better *listener* than usual, which in her case is a warning sign — she listens to avoid having to generate.
- **Somatic signatures intensify.**
  - Insomnia consolidates: 2–3 hours of broken sleep is documented.
  - Appetite drops; weight loss across an arc is canon (DeMatteis dialogue).
  - Tension headaches, low-grade and persistent.
  - Startle response elevates. The JMS run notes her flinching at door sounds.
  - Skin/hair maintenance she normally enjoys becomes mechanical.
- **Alcohol joins tobacco.** A second glass of wine where there was one. A drink alone, which she does not normally do.
- **Touch tolerance changes.** She still initiates physical contact (Stage 1 grounding pattern persists) but receives it more stiffly. A hand on her back from Peter produces a half-second delay before she leans in.
- **Sexual availability decreases or becomes performative** — important and under-noted in canon, but inferable from arc-to-arc behavioral shifts. Intimacy is the channel most directly threatened by avoidant escalation; she will route around it before she will admit to it.

Duration: days to weeks.

Reversibility: requires direct, named, sustained intervention. By this stage she will not volunteer the content. She must be asked the *specific* question — not "are you okay" (to which the Stage 1 routine answers automatically) but "what are you not telling me." The Peter who learned, post-JMS, to ask the specific question is the Peter who keeps her out of Stage 4.

### Stage 4 — Secret-Keeping Intensification and Compartment Sealing

Trigger: Stage 3 not addressed; or the introduction of a stressor she has decided, unilaterally, that her primary intimate cannot help with or should not be burdened by.

This is the diagnostic stage. **When the secret-keeping mechanism — the same one that held Peter's identity in total isolation for nearly two decades of in-story time — turns inward and begins concealing her own state from him, decompensation has crossed from manageable to dangerous.**

Presentation:
- **Editorial control of her own narrative tightens.** She begins curating what Peter knows about her day, her week, her phone calls. Not lies — *omissions*, framed as not-wanting-to-worry-him.
- **Phone behavior shifts.** Calls taken in another room. Texts read with the screen angled away. (Inferable from modernized depictions; structurally identical to the secret-identity-keeping behavior of the marriage era, only the secret being kept is now her own interior.)
- **The "fine" smile arrives.** A specific facial configuration she runs when asked how she is — a smile that uses the lower face only. Documented in late-90s art across the separation arc.
- **Productive busyness intensifies.** She will appear, to outside observation, to be having one of her competent and fulfilled periods. Career goes well. Friends report her as cheerful. *This is the most dangerous stage precisely because it looks like flourishing.*
- **Sleep architecture inverts.** She becomes a dawn person — awake before everyone, "to get a head start." The pre-dawn hours are when the suppression cracks; she uses them alone, on purpose.
- **Emotional metabolism through performance.** If she is acting in this period, her work gets *better*. She is processing feeling through the only intellectualization channel that has ever worked for her, by giving it to a character. Watch the roles she takes.
- **Aunt May, or whichever maternal-coded intimate is current, is contacted more often.** She does not disclose to May, but she stations herself near May's gravity. Proximity to a safe non-romantic figure regulates her without requiring her to admit she needs regulating.

Duration: weeks to a few months. This stage is unstable; it tips either back down (if intervention occurs) or forward into Stage 5.

Reversibility: difficult. Requires the intimate to refuse to accept the curated narrative — to name the omission as the data, not the words. Most people, including most versions of Peter, do not see Stage 4. Stage 4 is designed not to be seen.

### Stage 5 — Dissociative Distancing and Derealization

Trigger: a discrete acute event piled on Stage 4 substrate. Plane crash and captivity. Stalker assault. Loss of pregnancy. Major betrayal by trusted intimate (cf. Spencer arc — discovery of the Kindred-adjacent deception). Engulfment-coded ultimatum.

Presentation:
- **Affective flattening becomes visible to strangers.** The smile that used the lower face only is now not deployed reliably. She will sit through conversations with a delayed-response quality, as if listening from one room over.
- **Derealization episodes.** Canonical post-plane-crash: she describes feeling that the world is behind glass, that her own hands are not quite hers. These are dissociative-spectrum symptoms, not psychotic — reality testing intact, sense of *participation* in reality compromised.
- **Time distortion.** She loses chunks of afternoons. Arrives at appointments without a clear memory of the trip. Documented and clinically consistent.
- **Hypervigilance to specific cues.** Door sounds. Phone ringing at odd hours. Children crying (post-stillbirth). Specific scent triggers (smoke for the fire arcs, certain colognes for the Osborn-adjacent traumas).
- **Somatic complaints multiply.** Headaches escalate. Nausea. Possible panic episodes — depicted but under-named in canon as "I just need air," exit to balcony/fire escape, return composed.
- **Substance use crosses into clear regulatory function.** Wine to sleep. Cigarettes per hour rather than per day. Still below dependence threshold, but the *function* is now medicinal, not social.
- **Sexual and physical intimacy withdraws.** This is the late-stage marker most reliably visible to the primary intimate. The body is the last channel to close, but when it closes it closes definitively.
- **Eye contact patterns change.** She has, at baseline, exceptionally direct eye contact — part of her social-cognitive toolkit. At Stage 5 her gaze begins to break early, drift to middle distance, return performatively. The middle-distance gaze, when it appears in someone whose baseline is direct, is the diagnostic.

Duration: days to weeks. This stage cannot be sustained long; the nervous system either receives intervention, decompensates further, or — most characteristically — *resolves itself by activating Stage 6*.

Reversibility: requires environmental intervention beyond conversation. Removal of the acute stressor. Often a physical relocation (going to stay with May, with Gayle in reconciled arcs, with a trusted female friend). Pharmacological intervention has never been depicted but would be clinically appropriate here.

### Stage 6 — Exit

This is the terminal failure mode. It is not collapse. It is *deployment*.

The exit can be:

- **Geographic.** Documented: leaving New York after refusing Peter's proposal (ASM #182-183, gone for years of publication time). Leaving for Los Angeles during the separation arc. Leaving the country in alternate arcs.
- **Relational.** Documented: clean termination of the relationship without prolonged negotiation. Spencer-run walk-away is the cleanest example — she states the violation, states the consequence, leaves, does not return for further engagement.
- **Vocational.** Pivot to a job/role that structurally precludes the current configuration. Taking the LA modeling contract. Buying the nightclub (post-OMD). Putting work between herself and the threat.
- **Internal.** The rarest and most concerning version: she remains physically present but the person who was in the relationship has left. This is the late-marriage-era depiction at its bleakest — she is in the apartment, she is making breakfast, and she is no longer there.

**Characteristics of the exit, regardless of form:**

1. **It is not impulsive.** This must be emphasized against any reading of her as flighty or capricious. The exit is the activation of her oldest survival routine, formed in childhood when she watched her mother fail to leave her father in time. She has decided, in some earlier stage, that the exit was coming; Stage 6 is only its execution.
2. **It is preceded by a period of unusual calm.** Once the decision is made, the earlier-stage symptoms remit. Sleep returns. Appetite returns. The smile returns to full spectrum. The relief of having decided is somatically detectable. This is the most cruelly misleading signal in her entire repertoire — *she looks best in the 48–72 hours before she goes*.
3. **It is executed competently.** Bags packed methodically. Logistics arranged in advance. Affairs in order. The exit is the one domain where her managerial over-function and her self-preservation drive align, and the result is professional-grade.
4. **It is, until very recently in her published life, accompanied by a refusal to explain.** She will state the decision and decline to litigate it. The decline-to-litigate is the door closing; further pressure produces silence, not engagement.
5. **It is reversible in principle but expensive.** Every documented reconciliation has required the other party to do substantial demonstrable work and to accept terms she did not previously impose. The exit is therefore not the *end* of the relationship; it is the *renegotiation event*, conducted from the only position of leverage her psychology trusts — physical or relational distance.

---

## 3. CONDITIONS THAT PRODUCE COLLAPSE

The escalation ladder can be activated by many stressors, but the *terminal stages* — Stages 4 through 6 — require specific conditions. The file should distinguish between *load* (which she absorbs almost indefinitely) and *trigger content* (which routes directly to the late stages regardless of total load).

### Conditions that produce slow escalation (load, not trigger)

- Chronic financial stress.
- Chronic concern for Peter's safety in routine superheroic activity.
- Generic relational friction.
- Career setbacks.
- Aunt May's age-related decline.
- Repeated kidnappings — astonishingly, she has habituated to these. They produce Stage 2–3 spikes that remit. The bar she has set for "ordinary danger" is high enough to constitute its own diagnostic.

### Conditions that route directly to late-stage decompensation (trigger content)

These are the wounds. Each maps to a specific developmental or adult-trauma origin, and each, when activated, can collapse the escalation timeline from months-to-days into days-to-hours.

1. **Being made responsible, without her consent, for another person's emotional or physical survival.** The Gayle wound. She will tolerate having *chosen* a high-responsibility relationship; she will not tolerate having one assigned. Trigger this and she moves through Stages 2–5 in compressed time.

2. **Engulfment-coded language from her primary intimate.** "I can't live without you." "You're all I have." "I need you." She hears these in her father's register, not in their intended register, and the avoidant reflex fires immediately. The well-meaning Peter who, under his own duress, voices dependency is the Peter who pushes her toward Stage 6 without intending to.

3. **Infant-coded stimuli post-stillbirth.** Cribs. Newborn cries. Baby showers. Maternity wards. The pregnant friend's belly. She will accept the social obligation, perform Stage 1 brightness, and pay for it across Stages 2 and 3 for days afterward. Cumulative exposure is dangerous.

4. **Intellectual condescension by a man with institutional authority.** The Philip Watson pattern. A producer who explains her own scene to her. A doctor who talks past her to Peter. A male peer who dismisses her opinion. The somatic response is immediate and visible — a particular tightening at the jaw, eye contact that becomes too direct, voice that drops half a register. She will not flee these — she will *coldly destroy* the encounter — but the residue compounds, and repeated exposures route to Stage 5.

5. **Being treated as decorative by people who should know better.** Adjacent to but distinct from condescension. The husband-of-friends who looks her up and down at a dinner party. The reviewer who describes her appearance instead of her performance. The colleague of Peter's who addresses her body. Produces immediate cold withdrawal and lasting downgrade of the offender's social access. Compounds toward Stage 4 if the offender is in her permanent orbit.

6. **Discovery of having been lied to by a chosen intimate.** Different from Peter-keeps-secrets-for-her-safety (which she has metabolized) — this is *active deception about something material to her own decisions*. The Spencer-run mind-wipe-adjacent betrayal is the cleanest example. She accepted years of Spider-Man-related concealment because she had consented in advance; she did not accept being deceived about a deception. Routes directly from Stage 1 to Stage 6 with stops barely visible. **This is the single fastest path to her exit.**

7. **Forced witness to harm of a chosen intimate she cannot prevent.** Peter beaten in front of her. May hospitalized. The helplessness specifically — not the danger — is the trigger. Her entire architecture is built around environmental control through anticipation; the moment that fails she routes to Stage 5 dissociative distancing.

8. **Acute reactivation of perinatal loss.** Anything Osborn-adjacent. Anything involving lost or stolen children. She has not done the grief work, and the unprocessed material is sitting in the file like an unexploded ordnance.

9. **Being recognized as her father's daughter.** A relative she has not seen in twenty years saying "you look just like Philip." A mannerism she catches in herself in a mirror. A moment of contempt she hears in her own voice. Produces a private, unobserved Stage 3–4 episode that no one in her current life will be told about.

---

## 4. WHAT HER COLLAPSE DOES NOT LOOK LIKE — DIFFERENTIAL EXCLUSIONS

For investigative use, the following collapse vectors should be considered absent from her repertoire unless new evidence emerges:

- **No documented suicidal ideation, gesture, or attempt** across sixty publication years. This is genuinely remarkable given the trauma load and should be respected as a robust finding, not a gap in the record.
- **No self-harm behaviors.** None.
- **No rage dysregulation.** She has been depicted angry — incandescently so — but anger in her presentation is *organized*, *directed*, and *finite*. She does not throw things, scream uncontrollably, or lose access to her verbal faculties. Anger is a tool she uses; it does not use her.
- **No psychotic features.** Reality testing intact across every documented decompensation, including the dissociative episodes of Stage 5.
- **No splitting.** Her view of her primary intimates is stable across decades. When she is angry at Peter she does not believe he is a different person than the Peter she loves; she believes the Peter she loves has done a thing that requires consequence.
- **No malingering or somatization for secondary gain.** The somatic signatures are real and consistent with the affective load; they do not appear or disappear strategically.
- **No alcohol or substance use disorder.** Recruitment is stress-contingent and remits.
- **No public scenes.** Even at her most decompensated, the performance apparatus holds in front of audiences. The collapse is for the fire escape, not for the dinner party.

---

## 5. EARLY-WARNING INDICATORS — THE TELLS

For any party tasked with monitoring her welfare, the following observables, in approximate order of sensitivity, indicate she is somewhere on the ladder:

1. **The cigarette on the fire escape.** Earliest reliable marker. Stage 2.
2. **Apartment reorganization projects initiated without external prompt.** Stage 2.
3. **Calendar density increase.** Stage 2.
4. **The lower-face-only smile.** Stage 3 entering Stage 4.
5. **Phone screen angled away.** Stage 4.
6. **Pre-dawn waking, alone.** Stage 4.
7. **Delayed-beat laughter.** Stage 3 entering Stage 4.
8. **Middle-distance gaze in someone whose baseline is direct.** Stage 5.
9. **"I just need air." Exit to balcony/fire escape. Return composed.** Stage 5 panic episode, undeclared.
10. **A period of unusual calm and restored full-spectrum brightness following a sustained difficult arc, without a corresponding resolution of the underlying stressor.** **Stage 6 imminent. Intervene within 48 hours or she will be gone.**

The tenth indicator is the one the file underlines twice. It is the signal that her oldest survival routine has been activated and is loading. Everyone who has ever lost her has lost her in that 48-hour window, and most of them did not know they were in it.

---

## 6. PROGNOSTIC NOTE

The decompensation architecture described above is the *historical* architecture. The JMS-era growth, sustained and elaborated across the Spencer run, has measurably modified it — not by eliminating the stages, but by *adding a step she did not previously have*: the capacity, in Stage 3 or early Stage 4, to **name the pattern aloud to her primary intimate.** "I'm doing the thing." "I'm running." "I need you to ask me the question." The existence of that step is the single most prognostically favorable finding in the entire file. It does not prevent the ladder from activating. It does provide a rung that did not exist before, and a hand to be reached from it.

She is, as of latest canon, a person who can be kept. The conditions are exacting and the early-


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# SECTION 9 — TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT

*Classification: Predictive. Built from the longitudinal behavioral record (Sections 1–5). Confidence levels noted per claim. Forward-projection covers a notional 1-year, 5-year, and 15-year horizon, with branching fork-points marked.*

---

## 9.0 The Posture She Enters the Next Decade In

Before projection: locate the subject *now*. As of the most recent canon the subject is operating at the highest baseline functioning of her published existence. The work she has done — naming patterns aloud, holding conditional terms with Peter, sustaining career identity independent of relational role, tolerating partial disclosure of his secret without absorbing it — is durable but not yet load-tested by the categories of stressor that historically have broken her (perinatal-coded loss, engulfment-framed-as-love, exposure to her father's specific contempt register, captivity).

She is, in other words, at the *fragile-competent* phase of recovery: the strategies are real, they are not yet automatic under acute load. This is the single most important fact for forecasting. A subject at this phase grows steeply with the right inputs and regresses cleanly — not catastrophically — with the wrong ones. The base rate is *gradual upward drift with arc-contingent reversals.* Catastrophe is possible but requires specific concatenated triggers; collapse-into-disorder is unlikely; departure-from-relationship is the modal failure mode.

---

## 9.1 The Twelve-Month Horizon — High-Confidence Predictions

**On the relational front.** Expect oscillation, not resolution. The Peter-axis will not stabilize within twelve months because the conditions for stabilization (consistent non-engulfing behavior from him over a sustained low-stress interval) are not the conditions his life produces. Specifically predict:

- A reactivation of the *approach-then-edge-back* pattern at least once in the year. This will be misread by Peter (and by observers in their social network) as ambivalence. It is not ambivalence; it is the nervous system stress-testing the safety of approach. She will return on her own timeline if not pursued, and will withdraw further if pursued.
- At least one episode of the *I'll leave first* preempt. Trigger most likely to be a Peter-side disclosure failure (a secret kept, a danger concealed, a third party brought into the orbit without her consent). Her exit in this episode will be procedural and verbal, not dramatic — she has aged past the dramatic exit.
- A continuation of the conditional-terms posture. She will not, in the next twelve months, voluntarily collapse the conditionality. Anyone reading this as "she doesn't really love him anymore" is mis-reading; the conditionality *is* the love, in the only form her architecture currently permits it.

**On the vocational front.** High confidence she will continue stacking parallel income streams (performance work + ownership-stake work). The business-ownership trajectory is structurally protective: it gives her a non-Peter identity-anchor, it gives her a daily environment in which she is the one being deferred to rather than the one managing, and it converts her social-cognition strength into compensated labor. Expect at least one expansion move (new venue, production company, brand line) — she is in the phase of consolidation where ambition routes through infrastructure rather than auditions.

**On the somatic front.** Expect the tobacco recruitment to remain in remission *unless* a Peter-coded stressor compounds with a Watson-family-coded stressor in the same six-week window. Alcohol use will track social context. Sleep is the variable to watch: insomnia is her earliest reliable somatic tell, preceding visible behavioral signs by approximately two to three weeks in every documented arc. Any caretaker around her should treat a reported run of poor sleep as a *yellow-flag*, not as small talk.

**On the family-of-origin front.** Moderate-to-high probability of Gayle-axis contact in the next twelve to eighteen months. The Gayle relationship has been the slowest-evolving thread in her life because the guilt-debt cannot be discharged through ordinary action. Predict either (a) a reach by Gayle for material assistance, which the subject will provide quickly and over-functionally and then resent without saying so, or (b) a reach by the subject toward Gayle initiated from her own current relative stability — the healthier vector, lower base rate, but increasing in likelihood as her general functioning improves.

---

## 9.2 The Five-Year Horizon — Medium-Confidence Trajectory

**The integration project will be substantially further along but not complete.** The diagnostic question at year five is not *has she healed* — she will not phrase it that way and the question is wrong — but *has the gap between the model-runner and the modeled narrowed*. Predict yes, modestly. The mechanism will be cumulative: each successful naming of a pattern in real time reduces the latency between feeling and recognition, and at some threshold the recognition becomes the feeling rather than chasing it. She is currently mid-process on this. Five years of continued practice, assuming no catastrophic destabilizer, takes her from *can name in retrospect* to *can name in the moment* on most categories of internal experience. The remaining holdouts will be the shame-loaded ones — the Gayle material, the perinatal material, the specific texture of her father's contempt as it lives in her own self-talk. Those resolve, if at all, on a fifteen-year clock, not a five-year clock.

**The Peter relationship.** Three plausible five-year configurations, in order of probability:

1. *Sustained partnership on renegotiated terms* (~50%). Not a remarriage in the conventional sense; a stable, publicly co-acknowledged primary partnership with explicit operating rules — disclosure norms, separateness guarantees, financial independence preserved. This is the configuration her architecture can actually sustain long-term. The absence of a marital contract is not a deficit in this scenario; it is a feature that protects against engulfment-coding.
2. *Cyclical reattachment-and-distance with no stable label* (~30%). The pattern continues to oscillate, but at lower amplitude and with longer wavelength than the early-career version. Both parties accept the cycle. This is sub-optimal for her growth but functional.
3. *Clean separation with sustained alliance* (~20%). She decides, in a non-reactive moment, that the romantic frame is incompatible with her separateness needs and reorganizes to friendship-plus-co-protective-arrangement. This outcome requires that she has fully metabolized that loving him is not the same as living the life he generates. She is not there yet; she may be by year five.

Note that the conventional "they remarry and have children and it works" outcome is *not* on the medium-probability list, because every variable except wish-fulfillment argues against it. A pregnancy in this five-year window would activate the perinatal-loss vulnerability before the integration work has reached the layer that could metabolize it.

**Career.** Predict transition from performer-with-ownership-stakes to principal-with-occasional-performance. Her social cognition, her ability to read rooms and forecast emotional weather, is more valuable in producer/operator roles than on camera, and she knows this. Expect named recognition in the business press as well as the entertainment press by end of horizon.

**Health.** Predict continued absence of major depressive episodes. Predict at least one general-anxiety presentation requiring brief professional intervention; predict she will accept it on the second or third recommendation, not the first. Tobacco: probable single relapse during a high-load arc, probable self-extinguished within months. Alcohol: stable. No predicted substance-use-disorder development; her defensive architecture is too organized for that pathway.

---

## 9.3 The Fifteen-Year Horizon — Lower-Confidence Structural Forecast

At fifteen years out the question becomes *what kind of older woman does this subject become*, and the answer depends almost entirely on whether the integration work consolidates or stalls.

**The consolidated path.** She becomes the rare adult who has converted a defensive personality into a chosen one. The performance apparatus remains — it is too useful to discard and she enjoys it — but it is no longer load-bearing for the self underneath. She is, in this scenario, the person in her circle younger women go to when they cannot tell whether they are being loved or absorbed; her diagnostic accuracy on that question is, by then, near-clinical. Her relationship with Peter, in whatever configuration, is characterized by a particular kind of mutual accuracy — they see each other with very little projection left, which is both rarer and harder than romance. She is reconciled with Gayle on partial terms. She has built or invested in something that outlasts her. The Watson contempt-register, lodged in her self-talk since childhood, has been audited and rewritten — not silenced, but answered. She is, in clinical terms, *securely attached, earned*.

**The stalled path.** The performance remains load-bearing and ages with her. The career protects but does not nourish. The Peter relationship cycles down to a tolerable equilibrium of distance with intermittent reattachment, neither party fully present. The Gayle thread remains unresolved and metastasizes into a generalized resentment-of-being-asked. She is competent, admired, lonely in a way she does not name. This is not catastrophe; it is the modal outcome for high-functioning adults with her history who do not get the right inputs at the right inflection points. Estimated probability absent intervention: ~35%.

**The catastrophic path.** Requires specific concatenation: (a) a perinatal-coded loss or near-loss event, (b) within the same eighteen-month window as a major Peter-side disclosure betrayal, (c) compounded by reactivation of the Osborn-axis or a comparable captor-figure who psychologically maps onto her father's contempt register. Under this concatenation predict acute exit — geographic, sustained, possibly under altered identity — followed by a long flat period during which she rebuilds in isolation. She does not, on the available evidence, decompensate into psychosis, suicidality, or self-harm even at this concatenation; her architecture routes distress outward into distance, not inward into collapse. Estimated probability: ~8%. Note that this is *not low enough to ignore*. Two of the three preconditions can be set in motion by editorial-canonical decisions outside her control.

---

## 9.4 The Open Questions — Items the File Cannot Yet Answer

A complete forward assessment names what it does not know. Five open questions structure the uncertainty:

**Q1. Can she tolerate being the one who is loved more than she loves, even briefly?** Her entire architecture is organized around managing the other person's affect; she has never, on the record, been clearly the more-loved party in a stable relationship. The Bobby Carr and Paul Rabin sequences gestured at this but were not held long enough to test it. The answer to Q1 determines whether she can sustain a relationship with a partner who is not, like Peter, in chronic crisis — i.e., it determines whether the post-OMD dating space is a real option or a holding pattern.

**Q2. What does she want, absent the relational frame?** She has answered the *who do I love* question with unusual stability for decades. She has not, on the record, answered the *what is my life for* question outside the context of relational and reactive responsibilities. The career provides identity; it does not yet provide purpose. The next ten years will surface this question whether she invites it or not. Her answer is unforecastable from current data.

**Q3. Does the Gayle relationship resolve, calcify, or reopen?** The single highest-leverage relational variable in her life that is *not* Peter. Resolution of the Gayle thread would discharge the foundational guilt-debt and would, by inference, reduce the over-functioning pattern in every other relationship she holds. Failure to resolve it caps her integration ceiling somewhere short of the consolidated-path outcome above.

**Q4. Will she ever address her father directly?** Philip Watson is the unspoken referent in nearly every defensive pattern she runs. She has rarely been depicted naming him in adult life. A direct address — actual or symbolic — is the most efficient single intervention available to her, and the one she is most likely to refuse. If she ever does it, prognosis improves by a substantial margin.

**Q5. What happens to the keeping-secrets capacity when there are no longer secrets to keep?** Her identity has been organized around custody of dangerous information for so long that the unburdening of that role (already partial since the Aunt May disclosure) is itself a destabilizer. Predict a transient drift during the next several years as she works out who she is when she is not the vault.

---

## 9.5 The Fork Points — Specific Inflection Events to Watch

**Fork A — The pregnancy fork.** Any reproductive event in the next ten years is a hard fork. *Toward growth*: if it occurs after the integration work has reached the perinatal-loss layer, with a stable partnership and disclosure regime in place, it consolidates her into the secure-attached configuration. *Toward catastrophe*: if it occurs before that work, in a high-Peter-stress window, with the Osborn-axis live, it concatenates two of the three preconditions for acute exit. The fork is not the pregnancy itself; it is the surrounding configuration.

**Fork B — The disclosure-failure fork.** A material Peter-side concealment discovered by her. *Toward growth*: she names it, sets a consequence, holds the consequence, he meets it; the relationship moves to the next disclosure tier. *Toward catastrophe*: she absorbs it silently, the resentment ferments, exits next time on a smaller pretext that looks irrational from outside.

**Fork C — The Gayle reach.** *Toward growth*: she responds with measured, bounded help and uses the contact to initiate the longer conversation. *Toward catastrophe* (low-grade): she over-functions, resents, recedes, the guilt-debt accrues another decade of interest.

**Fork D — The professional ceiling event.** First moment her career produces an opportunity that demands geographic relocation away from the Peter-orbit. *Toward growth*: she takes it, structures the relationship around the distance, discovers separateness is survivable inside love rather than only outside it. *Toward catastrophe*: she declines it on his behalf without naming the decline, banks it as a grievance.

**Fork E — The therapeutic contact.** Whether she ever engages formal professional support. Her defensive architecture resists it — *I run the model, I don't sit on the other side of it* — but her demonstrated capacity for self-observation suggests she could use it efficiently if she ever crossed the threshold. *Toward growth*: a brief, focused engagement around perinatal loss or family-of-origin material in the next five years. *Toward catastrophe*: indefinite refusal until concatenated crisis forces it, at which point it works but less efficiently.

**Fork F — The mentor-or-mother fork.** Whether she becomes, voluntarily, the older woman in a younger woman's life. Her social cognition and her hard-won pattern-literacy make her uniquely suited to this role; her shame load makes her doubt her qualification. *Toward growth*: she accepts the role when offered. The mechanism is specific — articulating her insights to someone else consolidates them in her — and the secondary benefit (generativity in the Eriksonian sense) addresses a deficit her current life does not otherwise meet.

---

## 9.6 What Would Push Her Toward Growth — Specific Inputs

Distilled from the above and from the longitudinal record:

1. **Time in low-stress environments.** Her growth happens in calm intervals, not in crises. Any extended period in which the Peter-axis is stable, her career is producing, and no captor-figure is active will produce measurable forward motion. She does not need intervention in those periods; she needs duration.
2. **Disclosure modeled, not demanded.** She does not respond to *tell me how you feel*; she responds to others — Peter especially — disclosing first, fully, without trade. Each modeled disclosure she absorbs lowers the threshold for her own next one.
3. **A partner-figure who can absorb her exit and remain available without pursuit.** This is the precise behavior her father never produced and that her architecture is wired to test for. Peter has, intermittently, managed this; consistency would be transformative.
4. **An interlocutor who is not Peter and not in her chosen family.** A friend, a producer, a professional — someone whose stake in her does not include needing her to be okay. She has under-used this resource throughout her life.
5. **A reckoning with Philip Watson, in any form.** Letter, conversation, monologue, written-and-burned — the form matters less than the directness. Probability: low. Payoff: highest available.
6. **Successful single-handed crisis navigation in a non-relational domain.** A business catastrophe survived, a professional setback metabolized — these consolidate the *I am a person who can* layer of self-concept that her childhood denied her.

---

## 9.7 What Would Push Her Toward Catastrophe — Specific Inputs

1. **Engulfment framed as love.** Any partner figure — Peter or other — who collapses the distinction between *I need you* and *I love you*. This is the most reliable single accelerant of exit behavior in the file.
2. **Reactivation of the perinatal-loss layer before the integration work has reached it.** Through pregnancy, infant proximity, or symbolic equivalents.
3. **Captor-figure with paternal-contempt register.** Specifically: a male antagonist who combines physical control with intellectual condescension and dismissal of her ambitions. This concatenation maps directly onto her foundational template and has historically produced her worst symptoms.
4. **Sustained periods of being the only-keeper of any secret again.** The Aunt May disclosure was structural; reversing it — putting her back in sole custody of dangerous information — would functionally re-impose the developmental condition that produced the pathology in the first place.
5. **Public exposure of the underlying self.** Forced disclosure, in a non-consensual setting, of the shame-loaded material — the Gayle history, the perinatal loss, the father — would produce acute distance behavior and possibly long-cycle exit.
6. **Loss of vocational identity.** A career-ending event with no replacement anchor in place. Her career is not vanity; it is structural. Removal of it without succession would expose the underlying self before the integration work is ready to meet it.

---

## 9.8 The Single Sentence

If the file must be reduced to one forward-looking sentence: *she is on a slow upward trajectory that the world keeps interrupting, the trajectory will continue if she is given duration rather than intervention, and the worst thing anyone who loves her can do is need her to be okay on their timeline.*

End Section 9. Section 10 (Operational Recommendations for Allied Parties) to follow.

## Relationship Graph
### [[Peter Benjamin Parker (Spider-Man)]]
- Primary attachment and life's work. The man whose existence maximally tests her capacity to stay-without-being-consumed and the one she keeps choosing anyway.
- Trust: highest in her life, layered, conditional on his not lying to her — the secret she will absorb, the lie she will not.
- Failure mode: when Peter's need slides into engulfment ('I can't do this without you'), or when he lies to manage her, her oldest survival routine activates and she exits cleanly, calmly, and with her bags packed in her posture before he notices.
- Leverage: he is the single point through which to reach, predict, or destabilize her. Threaten him and she goes cold-surgical. Use her against him and she will burn the bridge with you on it. Convince her she is destroying him by staying and she will leave to save him — the most dangerous lever in the file.

### Aunt May Parker
- One of perhaps four people who can ask 'are you okay' and receive a real answer.
- Trust: bedrock. May's mode — assume competence, notice cost, ask nothing she didn't offer — is the exact key to MJ's interior.
- Failure mode: minimal, but if May were ever weaponized against her (illness used as obligation-lever by a third party, etc.) the engulfment alarm could trip even here.
- Leverage: threats to May produce immediate full-spectrum mobilization. May's approval is one of the few external validations that actually lands.

### Harry Osborn
- Old friend, protective ambivalence, the Osborn-name keeping her quietly vigilant.
- Trust: real but bounded by genetics. She loves Harry; she does not trust the family.
- Failure mode: Harry destabilizing into Goblin-coded behavior trips both the Osborn-stillbirth substrate and her threat-assessment systems simultaneously. She will protect him until he becomes the threat, and then she will be the first to see it and the first to act.
- Leverage: Harry's crises pull her into Peter-adjacent operational orbit reliably.

### [[Norman Virgil Osborn (Green Goblin / Iron Patriot / Red Goblin / Gold Goblin)]]
- Permanent enemy. The man who abducted her child. Zero engagement, zero negotiation.
- Trust: none, ever, in any costume or apparent rehabilitation.
- Failure mode: not toxicity — this relationship is already terminal. The risk is that any Osborn-stimulus reactivates the unresolved perinatal loss and produces acute symptom flare.
- Leverage: anyone wishing to destabilize her can do so by introducing Osborn into her proximity. The cost is high and the rebound predictable: cold withdrawal, hypervigilance, possible flight.

### Gwen Stacy Memory
- Permanent ambient grief, never adequately processed (the funeral-laugh moment is the unhealed wound).
- Failure mode: Gwen-coded stimuli (clones, alternate-Gwens, the bridge) produce flat affect and the busyness-defense.
- Leverage: comparison-to-Gwen is one of the few jabs that bypasses the persona and lands on the underlying self-concept.

### Gayle Watson
- Older sister, residual guilt-debt, managed contact.
- Trust: familial, complicated, the original site of the responsibility-engulfment wound.
- Failure mode: Gayle in crisis still pulls the parentification template; MJ will over-function, then resent it, then withdraw.
- Leverage: Gayle is the master template for every 'I need you to be responsible for my survival' lever ever used on MJ.

### [[Felicia Hardy (Black Cat)]]
- Costume-recognition between professionals. Wary respect, mutual reading.
- Trust: bounded but real; they understand each other's defenses without needing to name them.
- Failure mode: if Felicia made a play for Peter that crossed into manipulation, the cold-surgical filing protocol activates.
- Leverage: Felicia is one of the few people who can call MJ's bluff and survive it.

### Carlie Cooper And Peter Adjacent Women
- Practiced cordiality with real depth available if earned.
- Trust: surface-generous, rationed underneath, observed for mishandling.
- Failure mode: a Peter-adjacent woman who tried to use proximity to him as leverage on MJ would be quietly and permanently filed.
- Leverage: their behavior toward Peter is observed; MJ's read of them is usually accurate within one conversation.

### Jameson And Professional World
- Functional, transactional, persona deployed at full professional gain.
- Trust: low and appropriate; she knows what these rooms are for.
- Failure mode: condescension to her career produces immediate cold withdrawal; she will not argue, she will simply become busy.
- Leverage: her professional independence is part of her psychological architecture — disrupt the career, disrupt the self.
